Supervisors Held a Discussion Meeting Yesterday, Reporting on the Political Situation in Various Regions and Announcing the Central Work for Next Year 32

(Nanjing) At 8:00 am on the 17th, the Control Yuan held the sixth discussion meeting of supervisors. Those present included Yuan President Yu Youren, Supervisors Ding Chaowu, Fang Juehui, Dai Kuisheng, Miao Peicheng, Chen Zhaoying, Gao Yihan, and Secretary-General Wang Luyi, who attended as an observer. Yuan President Yu chaired the meeting. After the meeting began as usual, the supervisors first reported on the important work of their respective supervisors' offices, the political situation in each region, and the hardships faced by the people. Next, the Yuan President announced the central work for each supervisor's office in the 25th year of the Republic: (1) Pay attention to the progress of national economic construction in various regions and eliminate obstacles; (2) Pay attention to the advantages and disadvantages of the Baojia organization for the people; (3) Pay attention to the improvement of prison management and education in various regions, as well as illegal detentions; (4) Pay attention to the accumulated malpractices of tax collection agencies in various regions and those who are ineffective in investigating smuggling; (5) Pay special attention to the hardships of the people in border areas and find ways to alleviate them. Finally, the proposed motions were discussed: (1) Request the Yuan to formulate rules for the operation of the supervisor's office in accordance with the Organizational Regulations of the Supervisor's Office. Resolution: Passed and sent to the Counselor's Office for drafting, with Gao Yihan and Miao Peicheng participating. (2) Request a decision that supervisors' offices may assign secretaries, section chiefs, and staff members, in addition to investigators, to investigate cases. Resolution: Passed and submitted to the Yuan for approval. (3) Request the Yuan to issue a notice to the provincial and municipal governments that in the future, when compiling provincial, municipal, and county governance plans and changing personnel above the level of county magistrate, the relevant supervisors' offices should be informed to facilitate assessment. Resolution: Passed and submitted to the Yuan for approval. (4) Request the Yuan to advise the Executive Yuan to issue a notice to the provincial and municipal governments, instructing subordinate agencies to strictly comply with requests from the Yuan and the supervisors' offices to obtain documents and evidence. Resolution: Passed and submitted to the Yuan for advice and instructions. (5) Request the Yuan to stipulate the format of the response reports for cases handled by the supervisors' offices under order, and issue a notice to all supervisors' offices to comply with the reporting. Resolution: Passed and implemented by the Yuan. (6) Request the Yuan to advise the Judicial Yuan to issue a notice to all judicial organs that when the Yuan and the supervisors' offices investigate cases, they should provide full assistance when requesting legal investigation. Resolution: Passed and submitted to the Yuan for advice and instructions, as well as many other important cases. The meeting adjourned at 12:30 pm. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 11th)

Yongding River Water Rises Sharply 33

(Tianjin) The water level of the Yongding River is still rising sharply. The flood control gate in the Zhonghong dredging area has not been raised, causing the water to force its way into the new diversion channel in Tianjin County. Dozens of villages such as Zhao Family Village and Liu An Village in the north of the county are very close to the river and are in immediate danger. On the 17th, the villagers petitioned Tianjin County, begging for materials to urgently build defenses. The landlords of thousands of acres of farmland on both sides of the river also jointly pleaded with the county government to quickly prevent the danger. On the 17th, the county government forwarded the request to the North China Water Conservancy Commission for attention. (Special Dispatch, 17th)

(Tianjin) On the 17th, the water level of the South Canal rose again. The first and second sections of the Chang River reported to the River Bureau on the 17th that the water level at Lianzhen reached 16.29 meters, and the current was rapid, already level with the banks. The River Bureau has purchased materials, but due to delays in water transport, they will be transported from the Jinpu Railway on the 18th. It also ordered the three counties of Nanpi, Anci, and Wuqing to mobilize civilians to ascend the dikes and defend together. Zhu Baoqi, the director of the Flood Control Engineering Office, and others immediately set out to inspect. According to the River Bureau's investigation, the water rose due to the outbreak of mountain floods in Shanxi and half a month of continuous rain. The upstream Zhanghe River water rose and flowed downstream. Currently, nearly 300 villages along the river are in danger. The Hebei Construction Department remitted 5,000 yuan for emergency flood prevention expenses on the 17th and will continue to allocate funds. (Special Dispatch, 17th)

(Jinan) The main current of the Yellow River directly impacts the territory of Jiaocheng. The Kangtun civilian levee is being urgently reinforced. The Water Conservancy Commission has approved the purchase of two dredgers with 560,000 yuan from the Gengzi Indemnity to dredge the mouth of the Yellow River. (Special Dispatch, 17th)

The Hutuo River Dike Collapses in Raoyang County 34

(Tianjin) The water level of the Hutuo River in Raoyang County rose sharply by six to seven feet. On the morning of the 16th, the dike outside the county seat collapsed, and water flooded all four gates, cutting off all transportation. More than 40 villages were submerged. The embankment at Anpingkou on the north bank also collapsed at that time. Residents are making every effort to repair the breach. The province has ordered all counties along the river to mobilize civilians for emergency repairs. (Special Dispatch, 17th)

Financial Report at the Second Plenary Session (Continued from Yesterday) 35

(Nanjing) Regarding finance, Kong stated that in the past year, the economy was affected by the global recession and devastated by floods and bandits, reaching a low point. The industrial and commercial sectors were on the verge of total collapse. In the midst of extreme difficulties, the Ministry of Finance established the Industrial and Commercial Loan Committee and the Money Industry Supervision Committee, and allocated public bonds to provide relief to the market, thereby turning the tide. To stabilize finance and revive the economy, the legal tender policy was implemented in November of last year, with a reserve for the issuance of legal tender. Before the implementation of the legal tender policy, the total issuance by the Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications was more than 423 million yuan. By the beginning of July this year, it had increased to more than 861 million yuan, an increase of more than 440 million yuan in eight months. Part of this was to exchange for silver in the market, and part was to exchange for banknotes from banks other than the three banks. All issuance reserves are managed by the Issuance Reserve Management Committee and its local branches. Currently, the entire country, except for Guangdong and Guangxi, has uniformly complied with the policy and found it very convenient. Furthermore, due to the chaos of subsidiary currency, which harmed society, after the implementation of the legal tender policy, a subsidiary currency regulation was drafted and, after legislative procedures, promulgated by the National Government. The Central Mint was immediately ordered to cast new subsidiary currency in accordance with the regulation, uniformly in decimal units. Every time 100% of the new subsidiary currency is issued, one yuan of legal tender is reserved. By the end of June of this year, new subsidiary currency with a face value of approximately 8 million yuan in legal tender had been minted and circulated throughout the country. It is estimated that the number minted will reach 30 million yuan by the end of this year. Stabilizing exchange rates and consolidating legal tender are closely related. At the beginning of the legal tender policy, one yuan of legal tender had a fixed price with the currencies of various countries such as Britain, the United States, France, and Japan, which the three banks bought and sold according to. However, some who did not understand the truth said that we were linked to the British pound, while others said that we were linked to the US dollar. In fact, our currency system is autonomous and independent and is not linked to the currency system of any country. However, for the sake of facilitating international payments, there must be a certain exchange rate with the currencies of various countries to serve as a basis for calculation. Since the implementation of the legal tender policy, foreign exchange reserves have been extremely abundant, and the exchange rate has remained stable. We are currently in contact with the United States to purchase silver from us and provide us with the convenience of US currency at any time. With more abundant exchange reserves, the legal tender guarantee will be further strengthened, which is of great benefit to stabilizing finance, revitalizing the economy, and compensating for shortcomings. Furthermore, our country's banking system is not yet sound. In order to consolidate finance and promote legal tender, the government must adjust the banking system. For example, the percentage of commercial shares in the Central Bank has been increased from 40% to 60%. In the future, it is also planned to change it to a Central Reserve Bank so that it can be in a neutral position and become a purely financial center. As for other banks with special characteristics, such as the Bank of China, which develops international exchange, the Bank of Communications, which develops industry, and the Farmers Bank of China, which promotes agriculture, we are now urging these banks to develop separately in accordance with their responsibilities and are planning to establish a real estate mortgage bank to activate urban land finance. In addition, regulations such as the Banking Law and the Savings Bank Law are planned to be revised appropriately, and regulations such as the Land Bank, Provincial Bank, County Bank, and revised company regulations are drafted to establish a system and complete the banking system. Finally, Kong concluded that, in short, the financial foundation is built on the national economy. To ensure sound national finances, we must first seek the development of the social economy. Therefore, our efforts in the future should focus on production and construction and cultivating tax sources. Then, the social economy will develop day by day, and the foundation of finance will naturally be consolidated. Therefore, future financial policies should pay attention to five things: (1) save unnecessary expenditures and increase production and construction funds to enrich people's lives; (2) carefully select tax officials, strictly examine them, and eliminate accumulated malpractices to increase tax revenue; (3) rectify old taxes and promote new taxes to increase income and achieve a balance of revenue and expenditure; (4) improve the banking system and improve agricultural credit to facilitate the circulation of funds and promote industrial development; (5) unify the currency system and stabilize exchange rates to develop foreign trade and seek a balance of international payments. However, financial affairs are complex and multifaceted. It is hoped that all comrades in the party and compatriots throughout the country will work together to implement the financial reform program and achieve the goal of benefiting the country and the people. This is what we earnestly hope for. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 17th)

Domestic Goods: Measures for Transportation and Sales Licensing 36

(Nanjing) Regarding the "Provisional Regulations for Inspecting the Transportation and Sales of Imported Goods" and the types of goods subject to inspection, previously stipulated by the Ministry of Finance, a total of twenty-six kinds were listed, including rayon and alcohol. The Ministry stated that among these listed goods, some are manufactured domestically and are considered domestic goods. However, in reality, they are extremely difficult to distinguish from foreign goods. Therefore, these domestic goods are often detained when transported to various places, pending investigation into their origin. This situation is a significant impediment to legitimate trade and urgently needs to be remedied. The measures are now stipulated as follows: (1) When the domestic goods among the above-mentioned twenty-six kinds are transported through customs, the customs office shall issue a "Domestic Goods Transportation and Sales License." If the goods need to be transported to other locations for distribution after reaching their destination, the relevant trade association, chamber of commerce, or factory federation shall be notified to issue a "Domestic Goods Distribution License" based on the "Domestic Goods Transportation and Sales License" issued by the customs office. (2) If domestic goods are transported within the mainland without passing through customs, the relevant trade association, chamber of commerce, or factory federation shall be notified to issue a "Domestic Goods Certificate." On the 17th, the Ministry sent the above measures to all relevant agencies for compliance and implementation. (17th Central News Agency dispatch)

(Nanjing) According to reports, to avoid customs inspection of rayon imports, certain individuals are changing their methods, smuggling in large quantities of rayon components and blended rayon fabrics to evade customs interference. To prevent this malpractice, "Measures for Clearing and Inspecting Rayon Products and Blended Rayon Fabrics" have been formulated and will soon be promulgated and implemented. (17th Central News Agency dispatch)

International Commercial Telegram - Special Commercial News Telegram from Reuters, July 17th 44

Gold and Silver: London Gold Price: Today, the price dropped slightly by one penny, to 138 shillings and 10 pence.

London Silver Market: The market was calm today. Spot and futures prices both fell by 0.0625, to 19 pence and 625. India was buying and selling, while China was selling.

Mountly Silver: The market opened slightly weaker today. The December price was 45.05-45.25, down 10 pound音.

Exchange Rates: British-American: The London foreign exchange market was quiet this morning. The price of the pound was slightly weaker against the dollar. The British-American exchange rate opened at 5.0275, down 0.03125 from yesterday's closing rate in America and Britain. After an hour, it continued to fall by 0.0625, to 5.02875. The market situation stabilized later, and there were no changes at 1 PM.

Securities: New York: The market was very quiet today, but sentiment was stable. Most security prices rose slightly. Steel, oil stocks, and railway stocks saw the strongest gains. Buying sentiment was good later, but the gains were minimal. Steel stocks were firm, while copper mines fell slightly. The New York securities market prices are listed on the left.

Cotton and Wheat: New York Cotton Market: The market was weaker this morning due to favorable weather news for short sellers. However, it rebounded slightly due to purchases by the trade. The October price was 12.40 at noon, down 6 pound音 from the closing price.

Liverpool Cotton: Futures prices fell today due to favorable weather news for short sellers. The October price was 6.66 at 1 PM, down 6 pound音 from yesterday.

Chicago Wheat: The market opened firm today because the temperature in the wheat area remained high. Later, there were speculative sales and long covering. The September price was 106.125 at noon, up 375 from yesterday's net gain. However, it had risen by 1.25 points at one point at the beginning of the opening.

Chicago Grains: The market situation for mixed grains was the same as for wheat. The September price was 88.50 at noon, with a net gain of 1.5 points. It had risen by 2.5 points before noon, but the market saw a lot of profit-taking around 11 AM, causing the price to fall back slightly.

Liverpool Wheat: The market opened stable today, which was quite unexpected, as buying interest was good and sellers were unwilling to sell out completely. Later, the price rose rapidly because news about the American weather was favorable for bulls. However, trading was not heavy. The July price was 6 shillings and 8 pence 375 at 1 PM, up 1 penny from yesterday.

Rubber: London: The market was calm today. The October-December price was 7 pence and 75 at 1 PM, the same as yesterday's closing price.

New York: The market was stable today because the consumption report was favorable for bulls, which triggered speculative buying. The market situation was slightly quiet. The September price was 16.50 at noon, up 9 pound音 from yesterday's closing price. The New York commodity market prices are listed on the left.

Locarno Pact Nations to Hold Meeting in London, Opening on the 23rd, Italy and Germany Not Participating, Britain Striving to Avoid Pre-War Confrontational Situation 45

(Paris) The French government now agrees with the United Kingdom and Belgium to convene a meeting of the Locarno Pact nations in London. Belgium has also agreed to this. The meeting will open on the 23rd. Germany and Italy will not participate. (17th Reuters dispatch)

(Paris) The second Locarno meeting will be held in London on the 23rd of this month. The French government is no longer opposed to this, according to a confirmation by responsible officials. At that time, France will be represented by Prime Minister Léon Blum and Foreign Minister Yvon Delbos. (17th Havas dispatch)

(London) Regarding the Locarno meeting, some members of Parliament in the休憩室 (likely "restroom") recently stated that Britain now advocates that the UK, France, and Belgium hold a meeting in London, instead of in Brussels, and before the meeting, the three countries should issue a joint communiqué to explain that the goal of the meeting is to find ways to resolve various outstanding European issues. The text of this communiqué has already been drafted and is being sought after for French agreement. It is also heard that the government will send a cabinet member to Berlin to hold consultations with the German government in preparation for another meeting in the future, to which all relevant European countries will be invited. (16th Havas dispatch)

(London) The Locarno Pact conference was originally scheduled to convene in Brussels on July 22nd. However, since the British Cabinet did not make a decision on this matter yesterday morning, the date, agenda, and organization of the conference are still under discussion. The intention of people here is that, whenever the conference is held, its sole purpose should be to resolve European problems. This would be best achieved by a meeting of the five powers. If France believes that a three-power meeting should be held first to prepare for a larger meeting, then Britain should be persuaded. Britain is not prepared to participate in a three-power meeting that focuses on registering the failure of mediation efforts and does not have the goal of successfully resolving European problems. It is believed here that the formation of a Western bloc by Britain, France, and Belgium to confront the Central European bloc of Germany, Austria, and Italy is not conducive to peace. Yesterday, British Foreign Secretary Eden clarified this to the French and Belgian ambassadors. The Foreign Secretary stated in response to questions in the House of Commons yesterday that the suggestions drafted in London on March 19 by the signatory countries of the Locarno Pact, except for Germany, in preparation for the failure of mediation efforts, have not yet occurred. (17th Reuters dispatch)

Locarno Issue: Britain and France See Eye to Eye, Germany Will Issue Statement on British Questions 46

(London) It is generally believed that the Cabinet has not yet made a firm decision on whether to postpone the upcoming Locarno meeting. Political figures believe that the original agenda of the Locarno meeting was due to Germany's failure to reply to the British questions, and therefore the UK, France, and Belgium planned to take joint measures to respond. Now that the German-Austrian agreement has been concluded, Italy and Germany have become closer to each other. If the original agenda is maintained, Italy and Germany will cooperate more closely because of the close relationship between the UK, France, and Belgium. Therefore, if the Locarno meeting is held, its scope of discussion should be limited. In addition, the agreement concluded at the first Locarno meeting on March 19 stipulated that the general staffs of the relevant countries should discuss permanent measures to ensure the security of France and Belgium. Britain is afraid that if this is done, it will only further encourage Italy and Germany to become closer, so it does not intend to stipulate it. The Cabinet now instructs Foreign Secretary Eden to negotiate with France and Belgium based on the above views. The Foreign Secretary met with the ambassadors of those countries in the afternoon for discussions. (16th Havas dispatch)

(Paris) Regarding the objectives of the Locarno meeting, responsible parties recently stated that the French government holds the same views as Britain. What are the objectives? Namely (1) to study the general situation in Europe with reference to the agreement concluded between Germany and Austria; (2) to prepare for another meeting to be attended by Italy and Germany. After the current Locarno meeting is convened, it is imperative to devise the most appropriate way to conduct talks with Germany so that the situation in Europe can be clarified. It was also said that the French government does not currently wish to request Britain to implement the guarantees that the British government previously submitted to France and Belgium on April 3, stating the various measures that Britain should take to ensure the security of the two countries. (16th Havas dispatch)

(Berlin) Since Britain presented a list of questions on April 7, the German government has not yet responded. Diplomatic sources recently announced on the evening of yesterday that the German government now plans to issue a statement to respond to the British government. At the same time, it will also recognize the Abyssinian Empire established by Italy. (17th Havas dispatch)

(London) After the agreement between Germany and Austria was concluded a few days ago, political figures were originally worried that the close relationship between Italy and Germany might lead to various dangers, and were therefore uneasy. Now, this concern has been somewhat reduced. According to these people, the policies pursued by Italy and Germany, especially in the Balkans, are fundamentally incompatible. Therefore, the closeness between the two countries is only superficial. In fact, they only want to use each other to achieve their own goals. According to news from Rome, when Italy was using troops in Abyssinia, it had no time to take care of the defenses of the Brenner Pass, and secretly tried its best to help Germany and Austria conduct negotiations. After the end of the Italian-Abyssinian war, Italy still strongly promoted the conclusion of the German-Austrian agreement. Its intention is nothing more than two points: first, to show Britain and France that the Austrian issue cannot be solved without the assistance of Italy; second, to avoid the imminent danger of the merger of Germany and Austria. That's all. It is heard that Italy recently made another guarantee to Britain, stating that the country has always maintained peaceful intentions in the Balkans, so that Britain can cancel its mutual assistance agreements with the countries along the Mediterranean coast. This is the biggest obstacle for Italy to participate in the Locarno meeting. (16th Havas dispatch)

(London) Prime Minister Baldwin officially stated in the House of Commons today that Britain cannot agree to Germany's request to reclaim pre-war colonies. It is reported that General Pirow, Minister of Defense of the Union of South Africa, had declared to the press that Britain was prepared to consider Germany's request to reclaim colonies with a sympathetic attitude. Baldwin's statement today was made in response to this. (16th National Telegram)

(London) At the meeting of the House of Commons today, members questioned the remarks made by Mr. Pirow, Minister of Defense of the Union of South Africa, upon his return to South Africa from Britain regarding the colonial issue, and Prime Minister Baldwin answered them one by one. Members asked whether the government had formally discussed the issue of Germany's request to reclaim African colonies during its consultations with him during Pirow's visit to Britain, and whether it had made Pirow believe that if Germany made such a request in the future, the British government would treat it with sympathy. The Prime Minister replied that he believed that this questioning was based on misunderstanding. He heard that when Pirow returned to South Africa and met with reporters, he personally stated that the impression he (Pirow) expressed was the result of his private observations from conversations with individuals and groups, and not the result of special discussions with people in the British government. As far as the British government's attitude in its own country is concerned, he cannot add anything to what he said in the House of Commons on this issue before. Then Conservative MP Crowder and Churchill requested a clearer explanation. The Prime Minister replied that the government's answer could be said to be thorough and clear. As for the question of whether the government had made Pirow believe that if Germany made a request regarding colonies in the future, the British government would treat it with sympathy, he now answered no. (16th Reuters dispatch)

British Fleet Withdrawal, Gibraltar Suddenly Deserted 47

(London) As a result of the end of the Italian-Abyssinian War, the British warships withdrawn from the Mediterranean have successively arrived in domestic waters. The Escapade and Eclipse of the Fifth Destroyer Flotilla both arrived in Taiwan Port today. Those arriving on Sunday will include the flagship HMS Rodeny of the main fleet and five destroyers. After the withdrawal of the ships, the Port of Gibraltar has returned to normal. Five hundred port workers will soon be dismissed. Also, several cafes, dance halls, and clothing stores will be closed. (17th Reuters dispatch)

Draft of New Convention of Montreux Conference Completed, Signing Possible Next Monday 48

Montreux. The UK, Russia, France, Japan, Turkey, Romania, Greece, Yugoslavia, and Bulgaria have reached an agreement today as follows:

(1) Abolish the Straits Management Committee.

(2) Acknowledge Turkey's restoration of military facilities in the Dardanelles.

(3) Acknowledge commercial aircraft flying over the straits from the Mediterranean Sea to the Black Sea, but not over military areas. This new convention is expected to be signed on Monday. All countries also allow Italy to join afterwards, but the agreement will come into effect regardless of whether Italy joins or not. (16th National Telegram)

Montreux. The draft of the new convention on the Dardanelles and Bosphorus Straits, which will replace the 1923 Treaty of Lausanne, will be completed today and signed on Monday. Its contents can be divided into nine points:

(1) Merchant ships of all countries shall be free to pass, whether in peacetime or wartime.

(2) Warships belonging to neutral countries shall be free to pass, provided that Turkey is also a neutral country.

(3) Warships belonging to countries not bordering the Black Sea may enter the straits in peacetime or stay in the Black Sea, but only up to 30,000 tons.

(4) Submarines and aircraft carriers belonging to countries not bordering the Black Sea shall not be allowed to pass through the straits.

(5) Warships belonging to belligerent countries during wartime shall not be allowed to pass through the straits, except for those executing orders of the Council of the League of Nations or fulfilling regional conventions that Turkey has signed and joined.

(6) Turkey may arbitrarily prohibit foreign warships from passing through the straits when it believes there is a danger of war.

(7) The International Straits Management Committee shall be abolished immediately.

(8) As soon as the new convention is signed, Turkey shall be allowed to re-establish fortifications on both sides of the straits.

(9) Italy may join the new convention. (17th Havas dispatch)

Montreux. After the Montreux Conference passed the Soviet Russian amendment yesterday, the main points of contention were resolved. As for the critical issues, namely (1) the issue of the survival of the Straits Management Committee, and (2) the issue of aircraft of various countries crossing Turkish airspace, these two items were also successfully resolved after the General Assembly discussed them. The General Assembly, at Turkey's request, abolished the former, and for the latter, it decided that the places where aircraft of other countries are prohibited from flying are limited to the Dardanelles and Bosphorus Straits and the areas of the Sea of Marmara where fortifications are located. In addition, the General Assembly also decided that although Italy has not participated in the meeting, it can still sign and join it in the future. The General Assembly's discussion, which lasted until 10:00 PM tonight, has fully reached a compromise. The Drafting Committee is now putting the final touches on the draft of the new convention, which is expected to be completed tomorrow so that the General Assembly can be held at 3:00 PM on Saturday to pass the new convention. As for the signing period, it is scheduled for 3:00 PM on Monday. (16th Havas dispatch)

Czechoslovakia and Romania Announce Foreign Policy, Belgium Extends Military Service Period 49

Now that the German-Austrian agreement has been concluded, this economic organization will inevitably be easier to establish. (16th Havas dispatch)

All countries that can protect our country's and its allies' existing borders are allies of our country. As for our country's policy towards the Soviet Union, it is because that country has a population of 170 million, which belongs to a great power, so we should build good relations with it." Mussolini's Alarming Secret Plan: Five Measures to Transform the European Situation 50

(Rome) After the German-Austrian agreement was concluded, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini is said to be presenting an alarming plan to transform Europe when his vacation is over. Political figures recently put forward the following key points:

(1) Italian diplomacy is aimed at peace, and its purpose is to find a way out for the country's economy. There is no intention of expanding territory. As far as collective security mechanisms are concerned, Italy believes that their purpose is only to guarantee the security of France's borders, which is not comprehensive enough and cannot be approved by Italy.

(2) Italy is willing to cooperate with its friendly countries in Central Europe according to the original plan, but this plan is not to form a Central European group that is isolated from other countries in Europe. It will be different if other countries in Europe adopt a hostile attitude towards Italy. The various countries in Europe should also establish organizations around the Central European group.

(3) Italy still adheres to the principle that the countries of Europe should be divided into strong and weak, and is willing to cooperate with the strong countries. Regarding this point, it is generally believed that Italy has been in contact with Soviet Russia. Although Italy refuses to participate in the plan to encircle Germany, it also does not want to make friends with Germany alone. In addition, the second Locarno conference has been decided to be held first by the UK, France, and Belgium, and a five-nation conference will not be convened. Although Italian public opinion has expressed dissatisfaction with this, it believes that cooperation with France is still necessary. Regarding this point, Italy has issued a statement that it must wait for the mutual assistance measures established by the countries along the Mediterranean coast last autumn to be cancelled before it can participate. Since these mutual assistance measures have not been declared cancelled, Italy has reason to refuse to participate and should be glad. Prime Minister Mussolini believes that if Italy does not participate in this conference, it will be difficult to find a solution, and it would be better to postpone the date.

(4) The method of transforming Europe must be practical. In other words, compromise solutions must be established for all major issues. This can be seen from the agreement recently concluded between Germany and Austria. As for the reduction of armaments, it is actually impossible, so the countries concerned must limit armaments. The sanctions stipulated in Article 16 of the League of Nations Covenant should also be revised so that Italy can participate in the activities of the League of Nations again.

(5) Italy's plan originally intended to revise the treaties of peace of the European War, but political figures do not think so. They said that since Italy and Yugoslavia are in harmony, even though Turkey and Greece have both participated in the Mediterranean mutual assistance measures, Italy's current agreements with these countries are still valid. At the same time, Italy is also closely watching the development of Romania's current policies. As for Czechoslovakia, political figures did not mention a word about it. It is not yet known whether its policy is the same as Germany's policy towards Czechoslovakia. (17th Havas dispatch)

The French Chamber of Deputies Passed Two Important Bills Yesterday: Reorganization of the Bank of France and Nationalization of the Arms Industry 53

(Paris) The Chamber of Deputies today passed the Nationalization of the Arms Industry bill with 448 votes in favor and 85 against. The bill stipulates that the transfer of property of various arms factories can be carried out by the government purchasing shares at an average market price over the past seven years. The payment method will be through the issuance of public bonds. The Chamber of Deputies will also appoint an arbitration committee to resolve disputes arising from the transfer of property. (Reuters, 17th)

(Paris) This morning, the Chamber of Deputies continued to discuss the bill to nationalize the military industry. Right-wing Deputy Valentin proposed an amendment advocating that the government establish a permanent monitoring system instead of nationalization. The Chamber of Deputies ultimately rejected this amendment with 393 votes against and 164 in favor. (Havas, 16th)

(Paris) The bill to reorganize the Bank of France, proposed by Finance Minister Olivol, was recently passed by the Chamber of Deputies with a large majority of 430 votes in favor and 111 against. During the discussion, deputies from opposition parties expressed their opinions on various details of the reorganization bill. Subsequently, the rapporteur of the Finance Committee, Mr. Bruna, explained that the purpose of the reorganization was to change the administrative organization of the Bank of France to prevent it from being manipulated by a small number of large shareholders and to eliminate the preferential status enjoyed by those shareholders. However, the basic rules of the bank's operations and its powers regarding currency issuance, discounting, and lending will not be changed. The current reorganization bill is sufficient to achieve the above-mentioned objectives. Economically speaking, after the implementation of the reorganization plan, it is expected that the national credit system and the entire economic structure can be organized. Finance Minister Olivol then spoke, explaining the key points of the reorganization bill, stating that from now on, all shareholders of the Bank of France, regardless of the size of their shareholding, will enjoy the same rights and can participate in the election of directors (this right was previously limited to the 200 largest shareholders). After the reorganization, representatives from agriculture, industry, commerce, and labor will be able to join the administrative part of the Bank of France, and the position of governor will not necessarily be filled by a shareholder. Finally, Olivol asked the Chamber of Deputies to quickly pass the reorganization bill so that those who work for the welfare of the country can have their strength doubled to achieve success. (Havas, 16th)

(Paris) Finance Minister Olivol previously submitted a bill to the National Assembly, advocating that all funds owned by the French people and deposited abroad should be reported to the government with accurate figures before July 15th. Those who fail to report within the deadline will be severely punished. The Chamber of Deputies passed this bill on the 26th of last month, and the Senate also passed it yesterday. (Havas, 17th)

Details of the King of England's Escape: Thanks to an American Woman and a Policeman; Congratulatory Letters and Telegrams Pour in from All Countries; The King is Calm, the Assailant is Mentally Ill 55

(London) This morning, the King of England spent his usual life at York Palace. Before starting his routine work, he read hundreds of congratulatory letters and telegrams from all over the world. The policeman who knocked down the assassin's pistol, named Dick, also received many congratulatory telegrams. Dick served in the Navy and participated in the European War for four years. The name of the woman who discovered the assassin is still kept secret by the police. It is said that the woman is about middle-aged, and it is widely believed that she must be American. (Reuters, 17th)

(London) Regarding the assassination of the King, the first person to discover the rioter was a middle-aged woman in a gray coat. Although her actions are difficult to confirm, there is no doubt that she did something. After the incident, the situation was extremely chaotic. Some said that the woman was arrested at the same time as the rioter, but in fact, she was "escorted" to the police station by the police, and the chief of the station inquired about the details. Afterwards, the woman and a blonde girl left together, escorted back to their residence by police officers. The crowd cheered at them all the way, but the police station had made meticulous arrangements in advance to avoid passers-by asking questions. As for the woman's name, the police station did not announce it, fearing that after the disclosure, many people would come to express their admiration, which would make the woman feel uncomfortable. This woman in gray has thus become a mysterious and unpredictable heroine. (Havas, 17th)

(London) After the news of the King of England's escape from assassination spread, there were very significant expressions of loyalty throughout England. When crowded crowds gathered outside the palace, sincerely expressing their loyalty, the House of Lords also changed its traditional solemn atmosphere. After Privy Counselor Halifax announced the situation of the King's assassination, all the members cheered loudly and thanked God for the King's escape. In the evening, the audience and theater troupes in many theaters in London sang the national anthem "God Save the King". The only calm and composed person in the midst of the national surprise yesterday afternoon was the King himself. After the assassin was arrested, the King continued to ride forward as if nothing had happened. After the meal, he took a car from New York Palace to the Com Hill Golf Club to play golf as usual. When he returned to London in the evening, he went to St. James's Palace to handle government affairs. The first person to congratulate the King on his safe return to London was his mother, Queen Mary. This unexpected incident shocked the country. The British people initially expressed surprise rather than anger, because although the King had only been in power for a short time, he had already won the love of the people. At the same time, the King was already loved by the whole country when he was the Prince. Now, someone has assassinated him, so everyone is surprised. Then, they were relieved because the King was unharmed. It is said that the King's great-grandmother, Queen Victoria, also escaped assassination in 1862. There is also a very coincidental event, that is, Queen Victoria was assassinated five times in her life, one of which was only a short distance from the place where the incident occurred this time. The assassin is said to be a journalist. In the afternoon, the Campbell Police Court in Poole Street was presided over by Sir Campbell. The charges were illegal possession of weapons and intent to endanger life. The assassin was wearing brown clothes, without a tie, and was trembling violently. Because he was disabled, he had a slight limp and wore specially made leather boots. Detectives told the court that when the assassin was taken to the police station, he said, "This is the fault of Sir Simon (Home Secretary). I sent him a letter last night and called him again this morning. The King was not injured at all. I really didn't want to hurt him. I just wanted to express my protest." Before the trial began, a burly figure in a flannel shirt and carrying an umbrella entered the court and was led to the lawyer's seat. When asked for his name, he replied, "I am here to observe the trial in a private capacity." The presiding officer asked the defendant a few words and then ordered him to be detained for eight days pending further trial. The defendant had a lawyer to defend him. The detective presented the defendant's weapon as evidence, of which five chambers were loaded with four bullets, and only the highest chamber was empty. The defendant had a postcard of the British King's portrait, a newspaper, and two bullets in his pocket. After the presiding officer ordered the defendant to be detained, his lawyer stated that the defendant, in view of the news in the evening papers, wished to declare that he had no intention or will to assassinate. When the trial was in progress, a large number of people gathered outside the court, and the police station sent a large number of police officers to maintain order. The defendant was then sent to Brixton Prison by car. When he left the court, the crowd pointed and scolded him. (Reuters, 16th)

(London) After the arrest of Mahon, the assassin of King Edward VIII of England, his defense lawyer Coston requested the court today to investigate whether the suspect had a mental illness. Officials indicated that they could approve his request. According to reports, after the suspect was arrested, he spoke incoherently and denied that he intended to harm the King, saying that he only wanted to express a "protest", but he could not explain what he was protesting. It is reported that in mid-April of this year, the suspect used the name McMahon to sue Mrs. Erlsder, a famous opponent of the death penalty, demanding compensation for car rental fees of 67 pounds and 6 shillings. The case was subsequently dismissed, and the appeal was not allowed. At that time, Mahon shouted "injustice" until the court ordered him to apologize. At the same time, it is reported that the police station had already anticipated that an unfortunate incident would occur yesterday, so two detectives were watching at the place where Mahon lived. Sergeant Sanzi said that Mahon had a picture of the British King and a copy of the Daily Telegraph newspaper, with the words "Do I love you?" written on the newspaper. He looked very panicked. It is also known that he recently edited a "Humanitarian Magazine." The King of England did not care about this scare yesterday. Today, he still took a car to Com Hill to play golf. He only called Mahon "a fool". Everyone believes that after this incident, the police station will pay more attention to protecting the King's safety. However, when the King was not yet in power, he did not like plainclothes detectives following him, and he often deliberately avoided them. According to the Daily Express, the suspect's real name is Pennygan, 34 years old, Irish, living in Glasgow, and has a brother in Dublin who is a priest. (National Telegraph, 16th)

(London) Mahon, the assassin of King Edward of England, must have lost his mind due to a kind of anxiety. His statement in court that he had sent a letter and made a phone call to Home Secretary Simon proves that he was opposed to the Home Secretary. (Reuters, 17th)

The Ministry of the Interior Advises Provinces and Cities to Avoid Using the Word "Slave" in Official Documents 66

(Nanjing) The Ministry of the Interior approved a letter from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, based on a request from the International Representation Office, to avoid using the word "slave" in official documents and laws. This is because the Chinese characters for "slave" and "maid" are often used together in Chinese writing habits. In fact, the word "slave" refers to a servant, which is different from the foreign concept of "slave" (Slave) who is bought and sold and treated as property for life without freedom. In order to avoid misunderstandings in the international community, in the future, government agencies should not use the word "slave" in laws and official documents unless they are actually referring to slaves who are bought and sold, so as to correct international perceptions. The Ministry of the Interior has informed the governments of all provinces and cities accordingly. (Central News Agency, 17th)

Tragic End to an American Love Affair 71

Mrs. Cliden of Ossining, New York, was sentenced to death for poisoning the wife of her former lover. Today, she was carried to the prison execution chamber in a reclining chair and executed by electrocution. The female prisoner had been in a state of excessive fear for the past three days, and her whole body was numb. She did not even feel pain when pricked with needles. Therefore, she could not walk at the time of execution and was carried in a reclining chair. The prisoner, wearing a bathrobe and velvet slippers, passed by the cell where her former lover, Albert Legrotto, lived. Mr. Legrotto has also been sentenced to death and will be executed after Mrs. Clarke. He is currently awaiting his death. The female prisoner refused to eat before the execution, but Mr. Legrotto ate as much as possible and claimed innocence until his death. (Reuters, 17th)

Where is Hirota's Cabinet Going? (2) 81

— Jia He

Hirota, once he stepped from Kasumigaseki (location of the Foreign Ministry) into the Prime Minister's official residence in Nagatacho, changed his demeanor. He was no longer a docile lamb, obedient to the military in everything; instead, he acted contrary to the military and bickered with them. This was because the major issue of disciplining the military weighed heavily on the military's mind; because General Terauchi opposed the behavior of the young officers that could disrupt military discipline; and because Admiral Nagano rigorously enforced the navy's complete discipline. Therefore, after the cabinet was formed, it was not Hirota who was busy fulfilling his pre-cabinet promises, but rather the military who were busy with their own "internal stability work." In the army, figures responsible for the "February 26th Incident" were successively removed from their positions. Even General Honjo Shigeru, who had achieved great merit and was elevated to the rank of baron from a commoner background for his contributions in seizing Manchuria, had to retire from the Imperial Palace (resign from his post as aide-de-camp to the Emperor). In the navy, figures like Masaki Jinzaburo, who had echoed the radical fascists with the "national essence clarification issue," were removed from the navy by Navy Minister Nagano. At this juncture, Prime Minister Hirota, breaking with established precedent, ordered that the three chief officials—the chief secretary, the director of the investigation bureau, and the director of the legislative bureau—not be allowed to attend cabinet meetings. In this way, not only did he fail to fulfill the promises he made before forming the cabinet, but he also turned Yoshida Shigeru, the military's trustee, into his own subordinate.

As a result, a chaotic battle unfolded on the Japanese political stage between the bureaucracy, the political parties, and the military. Regarding the bureaucracy's attacks on the Hirota cabinet and Hirota's counterattacks, and the political parties' internal struggles against the bureaucracy and their open disputes with Hirota, I have already provided a general overview in the 25th issue of the Central News Weekly, and to avoid repetition, I will refrain from elaborating further in this article.

Hirota not only weakened the authority of the Cabinet Investigation Bureau but also severed the connections between the young bureaucrats in various ministries and the military. Interior Minister Toshi Oiso wielded a broadsword, eliminating those who had long been sympathetic to the military; using the pretext of "election violations," he arrested numerous assemblymen, causing those associated with fascism to tremble with fear. Even the renowned Kuhara Fusanosuke "went missing" because of this. In addition, he mobilized the national police to arrest right-wing activists. As a result, the military's external support was eliminated, and its influence inevitably diminished. These tasks were nearing completion when the special session of the Diet opened. The army also knew that the Diet was the organ that would judge them, and they had to grasp onto a weapon that could make the Diet members yield; that weapon was the "martial law decree." Thus, breaking the record of Japanese parliamentary history, the sacred Diet opened under the encirclement of guns and swords.

On the opening day of the Diet, a "reply to the Imperial Rescript" movement swept through the bourgeois camp, because, breaking with established precedent, the Emperor specifically mentioned the "February 26th Incident" in the rescript. The incident was a past fact, and it was recorded in the rescript, which was not surprising. The reason for the panic among Japanese property owners was to investigate the responsibility for the incident. The more earnestly this was pursued, the more inevitable pressure was placed on the military.

In his "policy speech," Prime Minister Hirota also pointed out that "this unprecedented and unfortunate event... its cause lies in the instigation of unstable elements both inside and outside the military." The only way to extinguish it was to "promote constitutionalism." The more constitutionalism was promoted, the more the military would be brought to submission. This was the goal of the propertied politicians, but whether it could be achieved was another matter. As a result, our Prime Minister Hirota earned the praise of the propertied Diet members. He not only boldly defended constitutionalism but also openly replied to Aso Hisashi of the Social Masses Party's question about "the correctness or incorrectness of the capitalist system" by saying, "I do not know its essence." Although Kazami Akira ridiculed this as "a response below the level of a middle school student," Hirota frankly told Hamada Kunimatsu: "Regarding the question of the correctness or incorrectness of capitalism, such as industrial control and liberalism... because I am not an expert, I lack such knowledge and have not done sufficient research." Before forming the cabinet, didn't he deny liberalism and advocate "a fresh start for all government affairs," wanting to reform the irrational parts of capitalism? Didn't he propose controlling the zaibatsu and thus earn the honorable title of "Control Cabinet"? Now, he has denied it all at once, no wonder the Asahi Shimbun said: "This can be seen as a bold response of self-negation."

Page 11

Guangdong Province, Eastern Han River: Chen Jitang's Troops Shorten Defense Line, Huang Renhuan's Troops Retreat to Meizhou Area, Li Yangjing's Troops Retreat to Huizhou Area 82

Youtou Correspondence: Since Yu Hanmou was ordered to lead troops back to Guangdong, the situation in the upper reaches of the Eastern Han River has begun to unfold. Yu's 123rd Division line extends from Nanxiong, Xinfeng, Qiannan, Dingnan, Anyuan to Longchuan, Xingning, Wuhua, connecting with Deng Longguang's division. These four divisions are the elite of the Guangdong army, so Yu's military power has increased. Chen Jitang then ordered the Northeast Han River army to shorten its defense line. Huang Renhuan's Fourth Army retreated to the corner of Meixian, Jiaoling, and Dapu. Chen Hanguang's brigade guarded Chao'an and Fengshun. The families of officers in each army believe that war in the upper reaches of the Eastern Han River is unavoidable. Last week, they successively moved to Hong Kong. Each time a Hong Kong ship sailed, the cabins were bought up by officers' wives. Everyone scrambled to buy Hong Kong currency, causing the value of the legal tender to plummet. People's hearts are extremely shaken. Currently, there are no formal troops stationed in the coastal counties of Chaozhou and Shantou, and national defense is empty. The Salt Police Regiment, which was transferred to Shantou last month, was reorganized into a Garrison Army, following the Ninth Division to Wuhua and Zijin, currently stationed at Qinv Lake, Laolong, and Heyuan, defending the upper reaches of the Dong River, cooperating with the Huizhou Third Army to prevent Yu's troops from advancing. The counties, districts, and townships in the heart of Chaozhou and Shantou rely only on guards and militia to maintain rear security. Remnants of bandits from the Min border in Zhao'an harass the territory of Rao and Pu. Shops in Huanggang, Fushan, and Qian Dong are closed. Cars on the Huangzhao Highway dare not travel. Remnants of bandits run rampant during the day, taking advantage of the situation to invade the territory of Chenghai. For the past ten days, wealthy families in Yanzao, Jingzhou, and Donglong have mostly moved to Shantou to avoid the bandits. Chaos and anxiety are now engulfing the lakes and mountains.

Si Lie Discusses: Central Government's Financial Relief for Fujian Province, Foreign Debt Cleared by Central Government, Domestic Debt Repaid by Fujian Province 83

Fuzhou Correspondence: Si Lie, the new Director of the Finance Department of Fujian Province, is scheduled to take office on the 16th of this month. According to Mr. Si, the crux of the financial difficulties in this province lies in the failure to balance income and expenditure, with a monthly deficit of 200,000 yuan. Furthermore, the heavy burden of historical debt has led to robbing Peter to pay Paul and a hand-to-mouth existence. The failure to effectively reorganize various taxes is also an important reason. He is determined to thoroughly reorganize after taking office, strictly defining the reward and punishment measures for each tax bureau, and eliminating embezzlement and corruption. On the one hand, he will request the Central Government to assist in clearing debts and strengthening the financial foundation. It is reported that the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Finance, after the Provincial Government Chairman Chen Yi's report to the capital, have clearly understood the financial difficulties of Fujian Province. They have already agreed that all foreign debts will be assigned to the Central Government for clearing, while domestic debts will be repaid by the province. They also agreed to issue short-term treasury bonds of 900,000 yuan for thirty-five years to supplement the budget deficit and to increase monthly subsidies from 300,000 yuan to 400,000 yuan. This new increase of 100,000 yuan will be used by the provincial government to bear the expenses of the 52nd and 56th Divisions stationed in Fujian. As for provincial taxes, in addition to salt tax, customs duties, stamp tax, and tobacco and alcohol tax, which are national taxes and directly collected by agencies established by the central government, the remaining local taxes are collected by the tax bureau. However, due to the incomplete organization and excessive redundant agencies, a great deal of public funds are wasted. Now, the Finance Department believes that tax affairs should be unified, and a special business tax reorganization office has been established. A special order has been issued that from this month, all types of special business tax bureaus will be abolished and merged into the special business tax reorganization office for unified collection. The ten types of taxes, such as pawn tax, furnace tax, and house and shop land tax, will be handled by the county collection office to save provincial expenses and unify power. The county economic and collection offices and treasuries were established on July 1. All local taxes are collected by the economic and collection offices and deposited in the treasury every day. Then, the treasury will divide the funds daily according to the proportion of various expenditures for political, educational, and construction purposes, accumulating deposits in the treasury to avoid the evils of misappropriation and confusion. If the county government has temporary expenses, it can borrow a fixed amount of activity funds from the local branch treasury for application, calculated at 1,800 yuan per month for first-class counties, 1,200 yuan for second-class A counties, 1,000 yuan for second-class B counties, and 800 yuan for third-class counties. Borrowing can only continue after monthly settlements and clearing. When there is a shortage of grain, the county magistrate and the local finance committee can issue notes to borrow from the branch treasury for assistance. (July 15)

Daishan Fishermen and Salt Workers Riot: Thousands of Rioting Fishermen, Several People Including the Salt Yard Chief are Killed, Riot is Suppressed After the Rioters Leave 84

Hangzhou Correspondence: Daishan Town in Dinghai County, isolated in the sea, is a fishing and salt production area in Ningbo, with a total of 20,000 households and a population of approximately 70,000. There are more than 200,000 coastal salt flats and more than 10,000 salt workers. Recently, the salt affairs authorities have actively reorganized salt tax revenue and prevented smuggling, reorganizing salt yards in various districts in eastern and western Zhejiang in stages. The first step is to implement the "fish and salt color change" to prevent fishermen from smuggling. The second step is to conduct "Shoujian Gong," requiring all salt production to be returned to the pile. The Daishan district has dispatched engineers several times to investigate and select sites to build public factories, and is discussing with the salt workers separately. However, due to the implementation of the "fish and salt color change" this year, the coastal fishermen in the area have repeatedly had disputes with the tax police due to minor reasons. In addition, this summer, there has been excessive rainfall, reducing salt production and soaring prices, with the selling price per dan rising from one yuan to between three and four yuan. The economic impact on fishermen has been significant. The general fishermen mistakenly believe that the salt affairs agencies are deliberately making things difficult, so they harbor deep resentment. On the 8th of this month, more than 1,000 salt workers from Daishan and local fishermen from Nanfeng Mountain gathered at Zifusi Temple for a meeting. Representatives from salt yards and cooperatives also participated. As a result, there was no excessive behavior. However, on the 9th, at a continued meeting, there was a resolution to seal the boards and stop sunning the salt to express opposition to the return to the pile. Some salt workers who did not agree had more than 100 salt flats smashed and houses burned. Subsequently, the Daishan Salt Yard Chief and Weighing and Distribution Bureau Chief Miao reported that more than 100 fishing boats from Fenghua and Taizhou fishing gangs (commonly known as the Red and Blue Flag gangs, famous for being fierce fishermen who killed the anti-smuggling battalion commander in the eighth year of the Republic of China), with approximately 1,000 fishermen, had joined in, carrying firearms and led by several leaders, plotting mischief. At 9 a.m. on the 13th, more than 2,000 people gathered again and convened a general meeting at Donghua Palace, resolving to use force to resist the return to the pile and preparing to riot and burn down the salt yards. Salt Yard Chief Miao immediately dispatched a tax police squad, led by squad leader Hu Bugui, to suppress them. A conflict broke out between the two sides, with gunfire and mutual attacks, resulting in deaths and injuries on both sides. Squad Leader Hu was killed on the spot. At around 3 p.m., the rioting crowd turned to the salt yards and surrounded them. The fishermen with guns were in front, and the salt workers were in the back. The tax police at the salt yard defended with live ammunition. Bullets and stones flew back and forth, lasting for about four hours. It is estimated that four fishermen were killed and the tax police suffered minor casualties. As a result, the tax police were outnumbered. At around 7 p.m., the rioting crowd broke through the back of the Weighing and Distribution Bureau, and Feng, a tax police officer, protected the salt yard staff and broke through the encirclement. The rioting crowd, in addition to smashing all items, set fire to all the salt yard houses. A small squad of tax police stationed at nearby Dongshazui was also surrounded and disarmed by the rioters. Salt Yard Chief Miao and Clerk Qian Qirong escaped to the home of a gentry named Tang. They were discovered by the rioters, who forced them to hand them over, otherwise they would burn down the house. As a result, Miao, Qian, and others were killed with stones and their stomachs filled with stones and sunk into the sea. More than ten staff members were killed at the same time, and more than ten were missing. The salt yard chief and each staff member's private residences were all looted. By the morning of the 14th, the burning and looting were completed. The rioters were still guarding the main roads, cutting off traffic. Therefore, no news could leak out. It was not until the fishermen boarded ships and left in the afternoon that martial law was lifted. Bei Shouwen, an engineer who was reorganizing the salt yards, escaped to Hangzhou on the 15th and reported everything to the Liangzhe Transportation Office. He said that this joint riot of fishermen had created an unprecedented tragedy. The Daishan Salt Yard's goods were also looted, with a total loss of more than 100,000 yuan. It is reported that the Transportation Office has separately telegraphed the Zhejiang Provincial Government and the Zhejiang Transportation Headquarters to dispatch teams to suppress the riot. It is said that the Provincial Government has sent security teams and the Second Squadron of the Water Police, and dispatched troops to cooperate with the Dinghai County Government to send personnel to investigate the riot.

Songjiang: Inspecting Trained Jia Heads 85

There are more than 9,460 Jia heads in the eight districts under the jurisdiction of this county. Training began on July 4 and lasted for 14 days, and was completed on the 17th. One day before the test, the seal was secretly broken and photocopied, and distributed at the time of the test. The seals were very strict. During the training period, County Magistrate Li visited various districts, and Commissioner Wang also inspected the training camps in this city every day, and was very satisfied with the serious handling. At 7 a.m. on the morning of the 17th, County Magistrate Li convened the trained Jia heads from the first district, Chenghuang Township, and held a graduation ceremony at Xiaojiao Field, inspecting more than 700 Jia heads. District Head Shen Fuyun and the heads of various townships accompanied them to the ceremony. County Magistrate Li gave a speech, reporting that the training of Jia heads was of great significance, followed by an inspection ceremony. After the inspection, Administrative Commissioner Wang Gongyu gave a speech. After the ceremony, photos were taken and everyone dispersed.

Suzhou: Bandit Robbery of Lanzhou Township Foiled 86

Lanzhou Township, Mudu, is located near Taihu Lake. Three bandit ships suddenly arrived the night before last, carrying ten, six, or seven bandits, each holding long and short guns. After landing, they broke into the homes of Wu Zaiqing and Wu Gentu in twenty batches, attempting to rob them. The villagers rang gongs and gathered a crowd, taking up self-defense earth guns to open fire on the bandits. The bandits also returned fire. Checking Account Books of Various Industries 88

The Wu County Business Tax Bureau previously sent a large number of staff to various shops to investigate the amount of business tax. However, because the filled-in estimated statements did not take into account the actual situation and were filled in arbitrarily, even differing by more than ten times, all industries opposed them and denied the estimated statements. They submitted the estimated statements to the County Chamber of Commerce and the County Chamber of Commerce convened representatives of various industries to hold a meeting, deciding: 1. Deny the estimate. Regarding the issue of checking accounts, if necessary, the respective industry guilds may send personnel to participate in the handling. Subsequently, after several contacts between Cheng Ganqing, Chairman of the County Chamber of Commerce, and Feng, Director of the Tax Bureau, a solution was agreed upon. The Tax Bureau will send personnel to jointly check the account books of the shops in various industries in the Chamber of Commerce with members of the Chamber of Commerce. The verification has already begun. Once the verification is completed, the first phase of the 25th year business tax will be levied.

Kunshan: Both Railway Bureaus Agree to Increase Runs 89
