Innkeeper Beats Maid to Death 90

Quan, who runs an inn in this county, had a maid named Shuangxi, who was only eleven years old. She had been in his service for more than four years. However, Quan was violent by nature and often beat Shuangxi, causing her injuries. The girl had no place to complain and could only cry in secret. Her situation was extremely pitiful. A few days ago, she was brutally beaten again for some reason and was on the verge of death. She died that night.

Wuxi: Silk Factories Scheduled to Resume Work This Morning 91

The problem of the Wuxi silk factory workers going on strike has eased slightly in the past few days. The county government originally limited the factories to resume work on the 17th, but the factories requested the county magistrate to postpone it by one day to resume operations on the 18th because the procedures were not completed and the internal affairs needed to be rectified. County Magistrate Long approved it. Regarding the provincial party headquarters, after reporting to the county party headquarters, a member, Zhang Gongren, was specially sent to Wuxi to mediate. After arriving in Wuxi, Zhang went directly to the county government to meet with County Magistrate Long to discuss solutions and instructed the committee members of the county party headquarters and the preparatory members of the General Labor Union on how to handle the situation. At 4 p.m. yesterday (the 17th), County Magistrate Long specially summoned representatives from each factory, four from each factory (two people in charge of the machines, two people at the head of the machines), to the county for a speech. More than one hundred representatives from 28 factories, including Ruichang and Yong, attended. County Magistrate Long gave an earnest speech: (1) All workers should resume work uniformly on the 18th. (2) The government will absolutely punish the rioters severely. (3) All workers should strictly observe local order and maintain social peace. Then, member Zhang gave a speech: (1) Labor and capital must work together to revitalize industry. (2) The Party and the government should help workers, gather opinions, and relieve workers' suffering. Finally, Sun Xiangfeng of the County Party Committee gave a speech, urging the workers to resume work, and put forward two suggestions: (1) To improve the treatment of workers, a trade union must be established to gather workers' opinions. (2) All workers should do their best to persuade the other workers to go to work and work with peace of mind on the County Magistrate's speech. All treatment and wage issues will be discussed and resolved after the Party and government agencies summon labor and capital representatives. At this point, the representatives dispersed. The county government has decided to mobilize fully at 3 a.m. this morning (the 18th) to persuade the workers. At present, the workers have agreed to resume work this morning.

Suppressing and Arresting Lake Bandits in Taihu Lake 92

Taihu Lake in this county is located between Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces. The lake surface is vast, and management is very difficult. Therefore, thieves hide in the lake and plunder everywhere. Residents along the lake cannot live and work in peace. In the past two months, the farming season has arrived, and local defenses are inevitably lax. Lake bandits have taken this opportunity to become active again. According to secret reports recently received by the Second District Commissioner's Office and the District Security Headquarters, a large number of lake bandits have been discovered in Taihu Lake, which are extremely rampant and acting at the right time. Commissioner Cang issued an order to the Muyi County Government yesterday, ordering them to immediately cooperate with the counties along the lake, send teams to suppress and thoroughly eliminate the bandits to maintain security.

Changzhou: Public Security Bureau Strictly Investigates Monks and Taoists 93

Tang, a native of Guandimiao Lane in Wuyi County, was recently defrauded by bandits. The first branch of the Public Security Bureau dispatched police in disguise and arrested Chen Bingquan, who was confirmed to be the perpetrator. He also confessed that he was a member of Chongfa Temple. After this case occurred, the quality of monks, Taoists, and incense keepers in temples has attracted attention. The Public Security Bureau convened a bureau affairs meeting on the 16th to discuss how to investigate monks and Taoists who come and go without a fixed place. It was decided that each branch bureau should strictly investigate according to the household registration book, together with the Baojia chiefs, to prevent criminals. In addition, Wuyi Buddhist Branch received a telegram from the General Directorate of Food, stating that in various places, there are often traitors disguised as monks, attempting to evade attention and plot wrongdoing. Not only is this related to the future of the monks, but it also has a great impact on national defense. Each temple should inquire about transient monks at any time, strictly investigate, and report any suspicious behavior to the local police office. The official office has ordered all temples to pay special attention.

Jiaxing: County Chamber of Commerce Organizes Anti-Smuggling Association 94

The Jiaxing County Chamber of Commerce believes that smuggling has been rampant recently, and Hezhou is a place with convenient transportation. A little carelessness can easily lead to smuggling. Merchants should take the initiative to organize a committee to confiscate smuggled goods, in accordance with the methods of Hangzhou. On the 16th, a first preparatory meeting was convened for various sectors. It was decided: (1) To recommend Jiang Fuqing, Yang Weisun, and Gu Suming to draft regulations. (2) In addition to the executive and supervisory committee members of this association, each industry guild should recommend two responsible representatives to participate as committee members. (3) To hold a second meeting at 21 a.m. to discuss and proceed.

Yangzhou: Boat Bandits Searched and Seized by Water Police 95

Ju Yuanlin, a villager in the Jiangjiazhuang area on the border of Jiangdu Sixth District and Taixian Kunsu, harbored bandits, causing bandit boats to dock there. Currently, local people have secretly reported to the second squadron of the first brigade of the fourth district of the Yiling Town Water Public Security in the Sixth District. The police were dispatched to search and arrest them and found two boat bandits. They immediately detained the villagers who harbored the bandits and transferred them to the brigade headquarters. On the 16th, the boat bandits were transferred to the Guazhou Fourth District Department along with witnesses. At the same time, the squadron was ordered to search for the remaining bandits to eliminate the source of the bandits.

Nantong: Various Industries Prevent Smuggling 96

Recently, smuggled goods have flooded the market towns in the coastal counties of Jiangbei. The Chamber of Commerce convened a meeting to discuss relief measures and decided to organize an anti-smuggling committee. In order to make it easier to achieve results, it was decided to convene a joint discussion of various industries on the 19th.

Water Level in Salt Canal Rises Sharply 97

Continuous heavy rains in Tongtai have caused the water level in the Salt Canal to rise sharply by more than one zhang. Cotton in the river is now suffering from flooding and weeds are difficult to remove. The dykes along the river are collapsing more severely due to wind and rain, and people are being drafted to prevent the intrusion of floodwaters day and night, causing flooding and disasters in Fanzhuan.

Changshu: Dongtang Suffers Seven Robberies 98

In the small village of Subin, Dongtang, seven houses were robbed in one night, resulting in heavy losses. The authorities are now in the process of arresting the thieves. The reason why Su Bin is a small village, where the residents are farmers who can make ends meet. The night before last (the 15th), more than 20 thieves from the mountains and lakes suddenly came to the area, speaking in the Jiangbei dialect. They first entered the home of Song Gengen to search for belongings. Because they were unsuccessful, they robbed Song Shengbao, Song Xiangsheng, Song Bingfu, Song Bingrong, Wang Xingzhai, Wang Xingzhen, and other seven houses. All of the rice, grain, clothing, bedding, etc. of each household were looted. Song Bingfu was severely beaten. The next morning, he was sent to the hospital for treatment. The losses in this battle were particularly heavy. The fifth branch office in charge has reported to the headquarters, requesting cooperation in arresting the stolen goods and thieves.

Giant Snake Struck Dead by Lightning 99

Recently, a giant snake suddenly appeared near the Xian Dongshishao in the southern suburbs. It was about ten feet long, all over red, with four feet, shaped like dragon claws, with whale markings all over its body, and moving extremely fast. It was terrifying. A few days ago, Yuanwen, the son (11 years old) of the nearby Dai, was bitten in the leg by the snake and died of poisoning. The villagers were very afraid and regarded Shishao as a dangerous place. During the lightning storm yesterday, a thunderclap struck the snake to death. For a time, the viewers were like a wall. The body was cremated with firewood.

Increased Grain Fields Throughout the County 100

Our county has grain fields amounting to, allegedly, 1.6 million mu. The Department of Finance also levies taxes based on this number. However, due to the lack of accurate measurements in the past, the precise number was never fully known, resulting in significant losses for the government. Recently, after land surveying and measurement, the area of grain fields has increased by over 400,000 mu. If the minimum tax per mu is five jiao, then the annual revenue from this county alone would increase by more than 200,000 yuan. Simultaneously, the total land area of this county is now known to be over 2.3 million mu, which is over 600,000 mu more than before the land measurement.

Huzhou: Tragic Murder Case in Shenjiawan 101

In Shenjiawan, near the Dahe area in the northeast of the city, a man named Shen Aji, who served as the deputy village police officer, was allegedly killed by a knife in the middle of the night the other day. He was on his way home from somewhere when he was attacked near a wooden bridge. The body was discovered by passersby the following morning. The deceased had more than ten knife wounds on his face, neck, and back of the neck, and he also sustained serious injuries to his waist. According to public opinion, some say he was killed due to an affair, while others say it was because he was too harsh in collecting land taxes, causing resentment and leading to this disaster. After the family of Shen reported the case to the court for an autopsy, the court ordered an autopsy and investigation of the murderer.

Taizhou: Militia Troops Encircle and Suppress Bandits 102

The Wenling County Government received a telegram from Liang Ding, the head of Xia Bi Township in the eastern district, at 8:00 AM on the 13th, reporting that over 100 bandits led by Zhou Zixiang had landed at Jinqing Port. The county government immediately dispatched troops to pursue and suppress them, ordering the 5th Brigade of the Henghe Township Security Team, the Jinqing Port Water Police, the Xinhe Tax Police, and the Eastern District Self-Funded Defense Corps to advance and suppress them. By 2:00 PM, the bandits were surrounded. The fierce battle lasted until 5:00 PM, resulting in the deaths of more than 80 bandits. The remaining bandits broke through the encirclement and fled. The militia troops are currently tracking and pursuing them. It is not yet confirmed whether the bandit leader Zhou Zixiang was killed.

This Week 103

— Special Dispatch from Beiping

Evolving Situation

In the past week, the situation in North China has shown significant changes. Because the Japanese side is completely ready on all points of personnel, policy, military, and economy, it has to require a clear solution in the near future. The consul general meeting in Shanghai and the three consecutive military attache meetings in Tianjin are a sign of this preparation. Therefore, Matsumoto Takayoshi, the deputy head of the Japanese garrison in Beiping, made a statement on the 10th, "Economic development in North China is beneficial to both China and Japan. According to the current situation, it is really necessary." He also said, "The politics of North China needs to be improved quite a bit. If the authorities are willing to work hard on their own, the Japanese side will definitely assist them." The so-called development is probably to be carried out by the Japanese side, and the so-called improvement is probably just to clarify the Hebei-Chahar political power and merge the Hebei-Shandong organization with the Hebei-Chahar political power.

However, at present, the Japanese side does not intend to take any steps militarily or politically. Its first step is still economic development. Under this goal, it exerts various pressures on the North China authorities. Of course, appropriate personnel are needed to cope with this very active pressure. Therefore, under the urging of both the Central Government and Song Zheyuan, Wang Kemin, who is familiar with the economic situation in North China, arrived in Beiping at 11:38 AM on the 9th. The Japanese side attaches great importance to Wang's arrival in the north and hopes to unfold the situation in North China from now on. Therefore, on the one hand, Japanese Foreign Minister Arita immediately sent an telegram to the Japanese officials here, "Absolutely assist," and on the other hand, Japanese tanks have been demonstrating between Tianjin, Fengtai, Beiping, and Tongxian for two consecutive days, as a means of both benevolence and coercion.

When Wang Kemin arrived in Beijing from Shanghai, it was rumored here that he would take over as the chairman of the Economic Committee of the Hebei-Chahar Political Affairs Commission. When he arrived in Tianjin, it was rumored here that he carried an "economic cooperation plan" in his luggage. However, after he met with the Japanese garrison commander in Tianjin, Tadashi, and with Song Zheyuan, Shimizu, Hanawa, and other Chinese and Japanese authorities in Peiping, his attitude here clearly showed that he was hungry. (1) The Chinese side is prepared to start economic cooperation with the Japanese side, but it must be beneficial to both countries. (2) The so-called economic cooperation plan is being discussed by the Chinese side, but there is no agreement at present. His visit here is just to inquire about the opinions of the Chinese and Japanese authorities here. Therefore, he will return to Beijing recently, and if necessary, he will travel between Nanjing and Beiping from time to time. According to statistics, Wang has stayed in Tianjin and Peiping for a week since arriving in Tianjin on the 7th. During this period, he had several banquets and talks with the Chinese and Japanese authorities, and the results were quite satisfactory. When he left Peiping on the 12th, he also made a very positive statement, saying that he would return to the north before the end of the month, and he would also consider the matter of the chairmanship of the Economic Committee at that time. Wang's trip probably made the attitudes of the Chinese and Japanese authorities here clear, and he will definitely report to the government authorities after returning to the south.

The Authorities' Support

External pressure is already enough to bear, and internal pressure is added with various declines and disturbances. For example, there are more than 380 stores in Tianjin that have closed down recently, and the general economic depression can be imagined. Therefore, the current expenses of the Hebei, Chahar, Peiping, and Tianjin local governments for the 20th year have to be reduced. Also, for example, Shi Yousan's wanted order has been explicitly revoked, and there are words such as meritorious service to the country in the explicit order, and recently, he will be appointed as a member of the Hebei-Chahar Political Affairs Commission. The difficult situation of the authorities and the painstaking effort to seek perfection can be seen.

After Chen Zhongfu arrived in Peiping from Guangdong via Japan, he immediately canceled his leave and resumed his position as chairman of the Foreign Affairs Committee. Zhang Zizhong, the mayor of Tianjin, had previously spread rumors of negativity due to the difficult situation, but after he came to Peiping for two days to report to Song and negotiate everything, he returned to Tianjin on the afternoon of the 8th to sit in town. All of this shows that the authorities in North China have reconciled much more in terms of personnel, and their steps seem to be very consistent. In particular, the resolution of the Fengtai and Tanggu incidents, from Song Zheyuan to all cadres and soldiers, can bear the burden of humiliation and respond calmly, and their intentions are also very admirable.

Regarding local security, around 1:00 PM on the 13th, the Public Security Bureau, together with the Japanese Police, went to No. 25 Zhengyang Street, Yantai, and No. 7 and 13 Liujia Hutong on the street to search and seize drug dens. They seized a total of 170 kilograms of opium and arrested seven principal criminals, including Korean nationals Zhao, Li, and Jin. For example, the capture of the giant bandit Liu Xiaohou, the imposition of the death penalty on repeat opium addicts, and the criminals who colluded with a certain country to forcibly occupy houses of the people are all manifestations of the authorities' determination to maintain social stability. Recently, Wu Enfu, the police chief of the western suburbs, was shot and killed while arresting bandits. When all walks of life initiated a donation to comfort him, Kurogen, the president of the Japanese New China News Agency, also donated ten yuan, which shows that even foreigners with vision agree with the authorities' determination to maintain law and order.

Recently, there have been various rumors about finance in North China. In Tianjin, the sudden circulation of 30,000 to 40,000 yuan of subsidiary coins in the market caused various anxieties. In Peiping, the discovery of a large number of counterfeit Chinese, Jiaotong, Hebei, and other bank notes greatly hit the credibility of legal currency circulation. In this situation of financial unrest, the authorities sent personnel to re-inspect and seal the silver deposits in Peiping and Tianjin to consolidate the credibility of legal currency, and at the same time, strictly suppressed the events that disrupt finance to protect the safety of the circulation of legal currency. Regarding the first aspect, Hu Yukun and others have completed the inspection and sealing. Peiping has 15,191,556 yuan in cash, and Tianjin has 36,978,000 yuan, totaling 52,169,650 yuan. Regarding the second aspect, on the 5th of this month, a large number of counterfeit banknotes and machines for making counterfeit banknotes were found at No. 3 University Alley, Jingshan East Street, Peiping, at the residence of Shu Jinghan, the military manager of Newell, a retired US Navy General who has returned to his country. The criminals Shu Runshan, Shu Jinghan, Wang Yunpu, and others were arrested. According to their confessions, they have made a total of 20,000 yuan in counterfeit banknotes. It is not yet known how this case will be handled, but at least it has dealt a great blow to the counterfeit banknote matter.

National Games Sends Letters to Chambers of Commerce Everywhere, Encouraging the Purchase and Use of National Goods 113

Since its establishment, the Shanghai National Goods Movement Federation has been making every effort to promote and encourage the use of national goods. Recently, in view of the fact that the market is flooded with private goods, the domestic goods industry has been greatly affected. It is particularly necessary to study and assist in the investigation. Therefore, the domestic group of the federation has started to investigate the production and sales of national goods industries. The first thing they started was the electric light bulb industry. The investigation results showed that although the domestic light bulb industry has made great progress in recent years, it has been greatly affected by the devaluation and dumping of foreign goods. Therefore, the executive committee of the federation passed a resolution to send letters to chambers of commerce in all provinces, cities, and counties to actively promote the production of light bulbs and persuade merchants not to be deceived by foreign merchants. These letters have been sent out yesterday. It is heard that the federation also has measures to assist various national goods industries in promotion. All national goods industries that are significantly declining due to the impact of foreign goods dumping may also request the federation to assist them. The original letter is recorded as follows: Dear Sir, I humbly believe that promoting national goods is the duty of every citizen, and the initiation and promotion depend on the advocacy of advanced members of society. Recently, the problem of smuggling has become increasingly serious, and the national industry is almost collapsing. In this extraordinary period, the responsibility of all individuals or groups who are enthusiastic about promoting national goods is particularly important. Our association is composed of national goods organizations in Shanghai. The internal parts are divided into three groups: domestic, foreign, and general affairs. According to the recent investigation by our domestic group, taking electric light bulbs as an example, the annual consumption scene is 17 million pieces, worth 8 million yuan. In recent years, domestic light bulbs have made rapid progress. Whether in terms of quality or effectiveness, they are not only comparable to imported products, but also have a tendency to surpass them. However, foreigners' economic aggression is meticulous. Foreign light bulbs on the market originally came from Europe and the United States, and are now manufactured in Shanghai. In order to concentrate their efforts and dump national goods light bulbs, they formed a joint business office. The dumping method is to repackage the substandard light bulbs discarded from old foreign brands and sell them with new brand names. The quality of the situation can be imagined. However, due to the particularly low price (from four jiao per piece to two jiao one cent), some compatriots are deceived by it and purchase and use it in large numbers. They do not know that due to its quality, it consumes more electricity and is often easily damaged, which is a loss. Domestic manufacturers and compatriots who purchase and use it suffer. Based on the results of the investigation, our association submitted it to the executive committee meeting for approval and sent letters to chambers of commerce in all provinces, cities, and counties to actively promote domestic light bulbs and persuade merchants not to be deceived by foreign merchants. I sincerely admire your chamber of commerce's leadership of merchants and the people, working hard in commercial transportation, and achieving great results. You are even more enthusiastic about the promotion and guidance of national goods. Therefore, I have separately listed the brand names of domestic light bulbs. I hope that you will carefully study them and ask you to inform merchants and the people not to sell foreign light bulbs again, so that the national goods can be preserved, and the national financial lifeline can be maintained. If you can inform us of the processing and the opinions on the quality and sales of domestic light bulbs, so that we can inform the factories to improve, it will be a public feeling.

Two Points from the Federation of Labor Unions Concerning Revision of the Income Tax Regulations; Instrument, Stationery, and Other Trade Associations Also Present Five Reasons for Tax Exemption 115

The Chinese General Federation of Industry and Commerce, yesterday submitted a document to the Nanjing Central Political Conference, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Finance, stating: "Yesterday, we read in the newspaper that the Legislative Yuan had passed the Provisional Income Tax Regulations. Upon careful reading, we believe that citizens have a duty to pay taxes, and if it does not harm the people's livelihood and benefits the national economy, there is no reason not to contribute. However, several points in the regulations have a significant impact on the people's livelihood and the future of industry and commerce. We have no choice but to implore your esteemed council and ministry to revise them. We respectfully submit the reasons, listed below: (1) Dividends from company stocks should no longer be taxed. Category 1, Item A stipulates that the income from profits of companies, shops, firms, factories, or individuals with capital of 2,000 yuan or more should be taxed at different levels. As shareholders are the constituent members of a company, the tax paid on the company's profits is actually levied on the shareholders. Now, Category 3 stipulates that interest from stocks should be taxed separately, which is a duplication. Individuals or partnerships who open shops, firms, factories, and do not issue stocks, the tax is levied on the profits of their shops, firms, and factories, and they cannot be taxed separately from their individual or partnered shareholders. The same profit, whether from individual capital or partnership, is taxed only once. However, companies registered in accordance with the law, in addition to paying income tax on their company, also have to pay income tax on stock dividends, levied on their shareholders. From a tax perspective, this is clearly a double tax; in terms of principles, it is also unfair. Furthermore, most wealthy Chinese people prefer to deposit their money in banks, and only a small number invest in industry and commerce. Therefore, various organizations in this city have requested to lower the interest rates on deposits to promote industry and commerce. According to the regulations of the income tax law, those who deposit in banks are taxed once, and those who invest in industrial and commercial companies, the company's profits are already taxed, and the stock dividends are taxed again. If the interest is deposited in the bank, it must be taxed again, totaling three taxations. Comparing those who deposit in banks with those who invest in industry and commerce, who will be willing to invest in industry and commerce in the future? Our country's industry and commerce are already in extreme decline, and even maintaining and promoting them is fraught with challenges. Now, imposing overlapping taxes is tantamount to dealing a major blow to the industrial and commercial sectors. (2) Savings deposits deducted periodically from the salaries of employees working in various factories should be tax-exempt. Category 3, Item B stipulates that the statutory savings of civil servants and laborers are already tax-exempt, and the savings deposits deducted periodically from the salaries of employees working in various factories should receive the same treatment and be tax-exempt. Employees who work in factories after being hired work hard all year round, equivalent to laborers, and their salaries and wages are mostly meager, far less than those of civil servants. Their usual income is often insufficient to cover expenses, and they have no savings. Once they lose their jobs, they are at risk of starvation. Because the current government has not yet implemented unemployment relief, various factories in the country have a practice of periodically deducting savings deposits from each person's salary and wages, paying preferential interest rates. This savings deposit is the result of frugality and is intended for unemployment or unexpected needs. Its situation is equivalent to labor savings deposits and more difficult than civil servant savings deposits, and it should be equally tax-exempt to demonstrate fairness. The above three points have a profound impact on the national economy and people's livelihood. We respectfully present the facts and appeal to your esteemed council and ministry to consider the difficulties of the people and grant revisions. We eagerly await your response. Sincerely, The Chinese General Federation of Industry and Commerce."

The instrument and stationery industry, the new drug industry, the book industry, and other trade associations in this city jointly sent a letter to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, stating: "We read in the newspaper that the Legislative Yuan had passed the Provisional Income Tax Regulations. Upon careful reading, we believe that citizens have a duty to pay taxes, and if it does not harm the people's livelihood and benefits the national economy, there is no reason not to contribute. Now, several points in the income tax regulations have a significant impact on the people's livelihood and the future of industry and commerce, and we have no choice but to implore your esteemed chamber to forward this to the government and appeal on our behalf: (1) Category 2, Item A, which taxes five cents for every ten yuan of monthly average income from thirty to sixty yuan, should be canceled. (2) Interest from stocks should not be taxed again as income tax. (3) Savings deposits deducted periodically from the salaries of employees and shop assistants working in various industries should be tax-exempt. (4) Income from author's royalties should be tax-exempt. (5) Compensation received from various insurance policies should be tax-exempt. The above five points have a profound impact on the national economy and people's livelihood. Our associations are deeply aware of the suffering of the people, and we cannot remain silent about what we perceive as dangerous. We respectfully request your esteemed chamber to forward this to the government and appeal for consideration of the difficulties of the people and grant revisions, etc."

Representatives of the Sauce Industry from Five Provinces Petition the Salt Affairs General Office Yesterday, Requesting Balanced Market Prices and Crackdown on Toxic Substances; Result: Permission to Thoroughly Investigate and Reduce the Price of Sauce Salt 117

The sauce industry from five provinces, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, and Hubei, petitioned the Salt Affairs Audit General Office yesterday because the Ministry of Finance had approved on September 4th of last year to crack down on tax-free toxic soy sauce, and to order salt merchants to balance the prices of sauce salt and edible salt. The order had been issued for a long time, but it had not been implemented. Therefore, the industry gathered representatives from various places yesterday to petition the Salt Affairs Audit General Office again. As a result, permission was granted for a thorough investigation, and approval was given to balance salt prices. The details are recorded as follows:

Representatives from Various Places Come to Shanghai to Petition

Representatives of the sauce industry from five provinces, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, and Hubei, including Wu Yinzhi and Chen Weiwen from the Shanghai Sauce Garden Trade Association, Fan Zishu and Wang Qingqing from Wu County, Zhu Ren'an from Songjiang, Zhang Bingjun from Wujin, Gao Yongni and Tu Xi from Zhenjiang, Liu Zhuyun, Cai Fengxiang, and Zhao Huiqing from Taicang, Mei Kuibo from Jiaxing, Fang Zhongfu from Baoshan, Ding Huchen from Wuxi, Tan Junyi and Jiang Dashi from Danyang, Wu Yongqing, Ling Zhenqing, Qiu Xie as representatives of the United Association of Sauce Industry Trade Associations of Zhejiang Province, Ru, Yao Ganqing, Chen Disun from Shaoxing, Ma Zhibi, Zhou Yiqi from Yuyao, Wang Youzhang, Shen Suishi from Ningbo, Chen Ronghuo from Zhenhai, Shi Zhechen from Nanxun, Niu Yansheng and Bian Juean from Linghu, Wu Jianqing and Shen Zihua from Xinshi, Shen Dade, Wu Shaolu, Lu Shoupeng, and Qian Wenbing from Changxing, Ma Shuliu and Ren Difan from Shuanglin, Ma Junming and Zhu Ziqing from Haiyan, Dai Songkou from Hangzhou, Wang Zhongchi from Xiaoshi, Huang Defu from Jintai, Qu Benhuai from Wuhu, Wu Rongli from Huaining, Wang Dongyou from Dangtu Xuancheng, Wang Wenchang from He County, and Zhai Yinting from Hankou, a total of forty-eight representatives, have all come to Shanghai to petition.

Request to Crack Down on Counterfeit Soy Sauce

The representatives arrived at the Salt Affairs Audit General Office of this port yesterday morning to request an audience with Director Zhu Tingqi. Zhu assigned General Affairs Section Chief Feng Ruliang to receive them. Because there were many representatives and it was inconvenient, Wu Kuanyi was elected to state the purpose and submit a petition, requesting strict punishment for the counterfeit soy sauce. The Ministry of Finance's order has not been effectively enforced due to the lack of appropriate measures, leading to prolonged neglect and aggravation. Furthermore, the raw material is saltpeter, which is intended for industrial use, and is now being sold in the same way as heavily taxed soy sauce factories. It should be taxed the same as official salt. If the current chemical tests show that it contains toxic substances, it should be strictly prohibited. Section Chief Feng replied that he would immediately transfer the matter for strict handling to maintain government orders.

Balancing Salt Prices Does Not Allow Ambiguity

Furthermore, the price of sauce salt is higher than that of edible salt by one yuan and three jiao and four fen per dan. The Ministry of Finance has ordered salt merchants to balance the prices, but they have not complied. Now that the national tax has been fixed (at seven yuan and two jiao per dan), the salt price should not allow ambiguity. If they still resist, sauce factories should be allowed to purchase official salt with the same tax rate from nearby salt warehouses to avoid manipulation by salt merchants. Feng replied that he would follow the instructions of the Ministry of Finance and instruct the Songjiang Salt Transport Deputy Office to strictly order salt merchants to balance the prices and prevent the sauce industry from suffering huge losses. The representatives were satisfied and returned.

Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs Will Extend the Limit on Flour Prices; A Certain Foreign Businessman in Hankou is Buying Wheat in Large Quantities 124

The Central News Agency reports that the flour market in this city was previously too volatile. In order to stabilize it, the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs specially set price limits for flour from near and far periods. Recently, the market has become calm, and there has been talk of lifting the price limits. A reporter from the Central News Agency inquired with relevant parties yesterday and learned that the authorities have indicated that they will extend the price limits. The nearby flour in the "July," "August," and "September" recent periods will be extended by seven cents, meaning that the highest price should not exceed three yuan and twelve cents. The far-term flour prices in "October," "November," and "December" will also be extended by one jiao. It is likely that official documents will arrive tomorrow or the day after tomorrow. It has also been learned that a certain foreign businessman in Hankou has been buying wheat in large quantities, causing the wheat price to rise, and the flour price will inevitably rise at the same time due to the rising raw material prices.

Sanctions Against Italy: China's Losses Are Not Significant; Customs Revenue Is Not Affected 125

After the League of Nations resolved to lift sanctions against Italy, our country also received an order to implement it and complied with the revocation starting on the 15th. The Ministry of Finance instructed the Jianghai Customs to implement it. A reporter from the Ta Kung Pao inquired with the Customs about the amount of trade losses between China and Italy during the sanctions against Italy. It is understood that our country's trade with Italy is not significant, accounting for a very small number, only about ten million yuan per year. Our exports to Italy are mainly cloth, tea, etc., while Italy's imports to China are mainly artificial silk, woolen cloth, etc. It is still difficult to estimate the losses since the implementation of economic sanctions against Italy, but it is estimated to be only three or four million yuan. There has been no significant impact on customs revenue.

Temporary Working Hours Issues: Ministry Approves Handling According to Law 126

The cotton spinning labor unions in the ten districts of this city have noticed that employers recently hire workers and give them temporary work permits. Even if they continue to work in the factory for more than three months, they are still regarded as temporary workers so that they can be dismissed at will. The factory law does not clearly stipulate the period for employing temporary workers, and it is difficult to negotiate. Therefore, on April 14, they submitted a request to the Bureau of Social Affairs to forward it to the Ministry of Industry to interpret the provisions of Articles 27 and 29 of the factory law, asking whether they can also be applied to temporary workers who continue to work in the factory for more than three months. Now, they have received approval from the Ministry of Industry (Labor Letter No. 4927): "Your report has been received. The temporary work permits issued by the Shenxin No. 1 Textile Factory in Shanghai do not specify a period. If the worker continues to work in the factory for more than three months, it can be handled according to the Interpretation No. 1155 of the Judicial Yuan. If the oral contract does not specify a period, the provisions of Article 20 of the Factory Law should be applied accordingly. In addition to instructing the Shanghai Bureau of Social Affairs to transfer the instructions to comply with the previous report, let it be known accordingly."

Jiangsu Provincial Government Orders Vegetable Cattle Inspection Office Not to Levy Transit Tax; City Party Department Has Already Instructed Ten District Party Departments to Be Notified 127

The Jiangsu Provincial Government has established a Vegetable Cattle Inspection Office within the jurisdiction of this city to inspect and re-verify the procedures for smuggled cattle transported to Shanghai from Jiangsu Province to facilitate inspection and re-verification. Unexpectedly, after the establishment of the office, it drafted a method for reporting cattle slaughter verification in the urban area, levied a per-head transit tax, detained cattle, forced donations, issued cattle driving permits for cattle dealers, and levied cattle transit tax. These actions hindered the effectiveness of the city's slaughter inspection and the city's issued permits, infringing on the city's jurisdiction. The Municipal Government repeatedly consulted the Jiangsu Provincial Government and ordered the bureau to handle it carefully and not to exceed the scope. Subsequently, the bureau replied that the Jiangsu Provincial Government had stipulated the office's task as inspecting and re-verifying cattle procedures, and had again ordered the office to comply and not to exceed the scope. After receiving the letter, the City Party Department has instructed the ten district party departments to be notified.

The First Special District United Association Forms a Citizen Training Association, Establishes Ten Implementation Measures, and Issues a Circular to Subordinates to Implement 128

Since the First Special District Citizens United Association elected to organize a citizens training committee and assist the government in promoting citizen training, they have established ten implementation measures and issued a circular to all subordinate district branches to proceed in a unified manner. Here are the measures: (1) These measures are formulated in accordance with the city's citizen training implementation measures and group training measures. (2) All members of the association and committee members of each district branch, whether members or not, aged 18 to 35, can register to join. (3) The training period is three months. (4) The training time is divided into two classes each day: (A) 6:00 am to 8:00 am, (B) 5:00 pm to 7:00 pm. There is no rest on Sundays and holidays. (5) For the time being, casual clothing will be used. It is even better if you can make your own uniforms. The common style is stipulated as grass-green military uniform. (6) The training courses are divided into political and military. The political courses are the Party, Citizens, New Life, National Situation? Red Bandit Crimes, and Overview of Rural Construction. The military courses are various basic subjects, and special courses may be added when necessary. (7) There is no fixed number of people, and the principle is to promote it universally. (8) Rewards and punishments are divided into groups and individuals. Those with excellent performance will be submitted to the mayor for rewards, and those with poor performance will be punished. (9) The report and implementation date will be announced separately. (10) Matters not covered will be notified at any time.

New Voice Society reports: Following the Shanghai Municipal Council's statement regarding Huadong (Eastern Shanghai) slum resident mediation led by Chinese Director Yu Qiaqing, slum representatives Wang Qitai, Sun Hankui, Tang Anping, Xu Xiguang, and others recounted the events: "On Tuesday afternoon at 2 PM, we went to Mr. Yu's office at the Sanbei Company. Submitted to the Housing Problem Committee for Discussion

Petitioning and Negotiating with Various Parties Again

Their letter to Mr. Yu reads: "Philanthropist Yu, we slum dwellers often trouble you. We feel deeply sorry because we suffer from having no money and no good jobs. We rely solely on our legs and hands, working all day long to earn a bowl of thin congee. That's why we build a shack to live in. Who with money would live in a shack? We truly have no other choice. The day before yesterday, thanks to your kind intercession with the Municipal Council, they agreed not to demolish our homes. We were overjoyed. But now, the Municipal Council has posted notices of relocation west of Haizhou Road. Upon hearing this, we truly feel lost. Whatever conditions, we can fulfill, as long as they don't demolish our homes. Alas, philanthropist, we are not guilty of any crime. Our landlords are not building houses nor designating relocation sites. Are they telling us to live on the streets, rob, or beg? Therefore, we have come again to ask you, philanthropist, to inquire with the Municipal Council whether they will demolish or require us to form a mutual guarantee association to avoid becoming wandering ghosts."

Yang Chong Takes Over the Golden Camel Company; Greatly Improves the Vacuum Pen 135

Mr. Yang Chonggao, the secretary of the recently dispatched Nanyang (Southeast Asia) inspection delegation, is a pioneer in China's vocational education sector. For years, he has presided over the China Vocational Guidance Center, contributing greatly to society. He has also consistently worked hard to promote the production and sale of domestic goods. Recently, he raised 50,000 yuan in capital to acquire the entire Golden Camel Fountain Pen Manufacturing Company, previously owned by Mr. Pan Qianxing, as well as all its vacuum pen patent rights. He renamed it the Da Wen Fountain Pen Factory, assuming the position of manager himself. He is manufacturing and selling Da Wen brand vacuum pens, whose quality has improved significantly compared to the previous Golden Camel brand, completely eliminating the ink suction difficulties. Currently, in addition to taking samples directly to various ports in Nanyang for promotion, Mr. Yang has also produced a large batch of finished goods, offering them at low prices to domestic stationery merchants for wholesale purchase. Furthermore, Mr. Yang, recognizing the increasingly serious unemployment problem among young men and women, plans to establish a fountain pen manufacturing technology training center. Within a short period, he will train them to become skilled in the technology and mass-produce Da Wen brand affordable and popular pens. They can then take machines home to work, and the Da Wen factory will pay them a monthly wage of 40 to 100 yuan based on their production speed. If this succeeds, it will provide another outlet for unemployed youth. It is also reported that although Mr. Yang has gone to Nanyang, regarding the wholesale purchase and inquiries about these fountain pens, you can send letters to the factory on Changping Road in this city, where someone will be responsible for answering them.

The house of Gu Asheng, a farmer in the impoverished village of Hujiatang, west of the Meilong Railway Station on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway, was in disrepair due to years of neglect and was dilapidated. A Lawsuit Regarding Inheritance Between Those With Different Surnames But the Same Ancestry; The Civil and Criminal Parts of the Xie-Qiu Case Are Both Concluded 139

De Qiu Rengao was previously sued by Xie Xien and his brothers in the First Special District Court to return a 50,000 yuan inheritance, claiming that Rengao was originally surnamed Xie and adopted the Qiu surname upon marrying into the Qiu family, and that he had issued a 50,000 yuan bond. The outside world has referred to this as a lawsuit between those with different surnames but the same ancestry. Details were published in this newspaper on the 1st of this month. After Qiu was summoned, he immediately sued Xie for obstructing his freedom. The Shanghai District Court sentenced Xie to a fine of 50 yuan for using violence and coercion to force someone to perform an obligation, with a two-year suspended sentence. Xie appealed, but the High Court rejected the appeal. Initially, the civil division of the First Special District Court ruled to suspend the proceedings because Qiu had filed a private lawsuit. Now that the criminal case is settled, the hearing was rescheduled. It was heard that the plaintiffs (i.e., Xie Xien, etc.) had applied to withdraw the case several days earlier, so the court did not open. Thus, the lawsuit between those with different surnames but the same ancestry is now concluded.

Shanghai Municipal Council Works Department; June Work Report 142

Shanghai Municipal Council Works Department June Work Report: This month, a total of 219 houses were under construction in the Public Concession. 197 requests were made for approval of building plans, of which 95 were approved. 82 houses were valued in preparation for requisition. A total of 5,767 inspections were conducted on houses. This month, the number of laborers employed on roads, ditches, parks, etc., totaled 5,235 coolies, 406 skilled workers, and 391 foremen. Furthermore, the amount of garbage removed this month totaled over 5,000 tons, which was transported to the east and west districts for land filling; over 2,000 tons were transported by contractors to other ports; and over 4,700 tons were transported to Maohai Road and Binlang Road for incineration. Furthermore, there were eight days of rainfall this month, and construction projects in various districts proceeded as usual without hindrance.

The Metal Industry Guild Re-elects Officers 143

The Metal Industry Trade Association held its third general membership meeting and re-elected its executive and supervisory committees on the afternoon of the day before yesterday. Over 40 members attended, including Zhao Xianji of Yufeng, Weng Jinglin of Tongyihe, Zhang Zuyuan of Shenji, Zhang Xingtao of Ruixinshuntai, Ye Xiangxing of Xinshuntai, Zhang Junfu of Yuantai, Xu Zhenbao of Zhengji, and Xu Peilin of Jiutai. Representatives from the Social Affairs Bureau, Zhang Dafu, the Municipal Party Headquarters, Zhu Yakui, and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Yuan Hongjun, also attended. The meeting began with a formal ceremony, followed by Chairman Zhao Xianji's report on the association's activities over the past two years and a brief overview of the 24th fiscal year's accounts. After distributing the report booklets and accounts, the Social Affairs Bureau representative, Zhang, delivered an address. The election then began, with Zhang Zuyuan counting the votes and Xu Peilin verifying them. The candidates with the most votes were Weng Jinglin, Ye Xiangxing, Shi Jiurun, Tang Luji, Chen Jinchen, Che Maozhang, Xu Shaomei, and Jiang Lixuan, who were elected as executive committee members. Mu Zixiang, Zhang Zhixing, Xu Peilin, Ge Wenjun, and Fang Guojin were elected as alternate executive committee members. Zhao Xianji and Zhang Zuyuan were elected as supervisory committee members, and Zhang Xingtao and Li Runsheng were elected as alternate supervisory committee members. They then took the oath of office. Continuing executive committee members Zhang Lianfang, Xu Zhenbao, Qiu Shaoxiu, He Guorui, Zhang Junfu, Chen Xien, and Ying Rulian, and continuing supervisory committee members Ye Xiangang, Cheng Lanting, and Liu Chunhua remained in their positions. At the end, the chairman announced that the outgoing executive committee had proposed six motions, which were passed by the general membership meeting: (1) Establish a finance committee. Passed as proposed, to be handled by the executive committee. (2) During the membership recruitment period, change the three types of membership fees stipulated in the association's constitution. The original fees were 600 yuan for Class A, changed to 400 yuan; 300 yuan for Class B, changed to 200 yuan; and 150 yuan for Class C, changed to 100 yuan. Passed as proposed, effective from August 1st to the end of October (three months), and all those in the industry are requested to join as soon as possible. (3) Member Xin Shun Ji requested that the business hours for the industry be set at 8 AM to 6 PM daily, and 8 AM to 12 PM on Sundays, with the afternoon off. It was decided to have no regulations on weekdays and to have the afternoon off on Sundays. A vote was taken, and the result was 25 votes in favor and 15 votes against, deciding that the afternoon off on Sundays would be implemented. The implementation date and method will be decided by the executive committee and announced in the newspaper. (4) Member Heng Da Xiang, represented by Zhang Lianfang, proposed that a mutual assistance association for metal industry colleagues should be established. Passed unanimously, and the details will be discussed by the executive committee. (5) The warehouse regulations should be revised. Passed to be revised by the executive committee and distributed to all members for compliance. (6) Procedures for paying membership fees must be established. Passed to be handled by the finance group. The meeting adjourned at 6 PM. Yesterday afternoon, the third first executive committee meeting was held, and standing committee members and a chairman were elected. Because Chairman Zhao had served for two years and had achieved considerable success in association affairs, and his term had now expired, Zhang Lianfang was elected as the new chairman, and Xu Zhenbao, Weng Jinglin, Qiu Shaoxiu, and Ye Xiangxing were elected as standing committee members. Xu Zhenbao and Ye Xiangxing were appointed to the General Affairs Section, and Weng Jinglin and Qiu Shaoxiu were appointed to the Finance Section. The meeting then adjourned.

The Case of the Son of a Policeman Drowning; Zhan Wei is Released on Bail 144

Yang Bingsheng, the 16-year-old son of Yang Dianchen, a policeman at the First Branch of the Shanghai County Public Security Bureau, was learning a trade at the Feilong Motor Vehicle Shop in Minhang Town. On the evening of the 11th of this month at 9 PM, he was cooling off by the railing of the Minhang ferry terminal of the Highway Administration Office of the Construction Department when he fell asleep and suddenly fell into the river and died. According to Yang's report to the District Court, he was kicked and killed by the administrator Zhan Wei. However, the inspector of the District Court determined that Yang Bingsheng fell into the river and died after being injured, and filled out the coroner's report accordingly. Yesterday, Prosecutor Zhao Chuanjia summoned the defendant Zhan Wei, the deceased's father Yang Dianchen, and witness Zheng Afu to court for a preliminary hearing. Zhan Wei claimed that the deceased had fallen into the river and died carelessly, while Yang Dianchen claimed that the defendant had abused his power and authority and drove his son into the river after seeing him cooling off at the terminal. Witness Zheng Afu testified to everything. The judge ordered Zhan Wei to provide a reliable business guarantor and await investigation and legal action.

Japanese Merchants Plan to Establish Two Datta Factories; Ozaki 1 Million, Samsung 2.5 Million; Factory Sites Have Been Located and Will Open After Completion of Setup 146

According to Da Gong She, the Chinese pigment market has been monopolized by Germany and the United Kingdom in recent years. Recently, two Japanese pigment companies with medium capital have been trying to restore their position in the Chinese pigment market and avoid China's 100% ad valorem people's tax by establishing branches in Shanghai to manufacture vulcanized black and water blue. One is the Oazaki Dyeing and Weaving Company, with a capital of 1,000,000 yuan, which has a factory in Osaka. The other is the Hiroshima Prefecture Samsung Pigment Company, with a capital of 2,500,000 yuan. In addition to the above two factories, the Japanese Pigment Manufacturing Factory, known as the most natural pigment factory in Japan and with a capital of 5,000,000 yuan, also plans to establish a branch in China to manufacture various pigments. The Ozaki Weaving Company recently took over a Chinese chemical industrial factory in Shanghai and is now installing equipment to manufacture vulcanized black and water blue. This new factory will operate as an independent company, named the De Kang Pigment Factory, with the aim of supplying the needs of various textile companies in central China. The Samsung Pigment Company has also purchased a factory owned by a Chinese businessman in Shanghai and established the Sanhe Pigment Engineering Company, which is jointly operated by Chinese merchants and the well-known Osaka pigment merchant Miki Shoten. The Sanji Company is in charge of the engineering technology, while the capital is raised by Chinese merchants and Miki Shoten. This company will mainly specialize in the manufacture of vulcanized black.

Pirates Abound Outside Wusong Estuary; Fishing Boats Robbed in Broad Daylight 147

Pirates have become rampant outside the Wusong Sanjiashui Estuary, with frequent reports of robberies of pig boats and fishing boats. The other day, the Ningbo fishing boat "Jin Tong Hua," Customs Seal No. 1432, was transporting miscellaneous goods from Hankou to Shanghai. The boat arrived at the sea area opposite Jiangbei New Port on the afternoon of the day before yesterday when it was suddenly encountered by a pirate ship. The pirates fired two shots as a warning, forcing the boat to stop. Eleven pirates, armed with five rifles, swarmed onto the boat, first confining the crew in a cabin, using the plaster of Paris that was loaded on board to hold them down and prevent them from moving, and then began to loot. They took 29 pieces of tung oil, two cans of camphor oil, five pieces of piqiao wood, seven pieces of hemp, and 160 yuan in cash, as well as dozens of pieces of clothing. The total loss was estimated at around 2,000 yuan. Afterwards, the fishing boat owner reported the incident to the Third District Water Police of Nantong and requested an investigation. The boat arrived in Song yesterday and reported the incident to the Xia Senji Customs Brokerage to request that it be reported to the Jianghai Customs and other agencies to request that the stolen goods be recovered and the pirates brought to justice. It is heard that the tung oil that was robbed was marked with the Chun Yuan brand and belonged to the Ningbo Changyuan Xiehao. Anyone who finds the goods and reports it to Xia Senji will be rewarded.

Continuous Wind and Rain; More Than the Same Period Last Year 148

The city has been experiencing continuous strong winds and heavy rain, and the weather is similar to late autumn. Yesterday afternoon, it was dark for half an hour, followed by a downpour. An hour later, the rain eased slightly. Overall, the weather from morning to dusk yesterday was rainy, and the temperature was cooler than the day before. The Huangpu River surface was hit by wind and waves, causing the river water to backflow, and water accumulated to a foot deep in low-lying areas on the roads. Shanghai's export cargo ships were greatly affected. Goods such as piece goods, yarn, sugar, paper, and cigarettes, which were scheduled to be loaded and transported to various ports along the Yangtze River, were temporarily halted due to fears of being soaked by the heavy rain. Some cargo was delayed due to the inability of dockworkers to load the ships. North-South Ocean, Small Yangtze, and Ningbo ships were also subject to the same obstruction. The number of outbound passengers on each ship was greatly reduced. Overall, in the past two days, cargo transportation on the Jianghai routes has decreased by 60%, and the number of passengers has decreased by half. The shipping industry is quite distressed. According to news from the Observatory yesterday, rainfall this year is higher than the same period last year. The amount of rainfall from January 1st to 12 PM on the 16th of this month has been 599.8 millimeters. The rainfall yesterday is not included. Last year, the amount of rainfall during the same period was 547.8 millimeters, which is 52 millimeters less. (Note that last year's rainfall was more than the same period the year before.) If the weather does not clear up, agricultural crops will likely suffer.

Methods for Foreign Cars Driving into Shanghai to Obtain Permits from the Two Concessions; Car Owners Must Pay a Security Deposit of 20 Yuan 151

Regarding the matter of foreign cars entering Shanghai and obtaining temporary permits from the concessions, according to the news released by the Shanghai Municipal Council of the Public Concession, the police and transportation authorities of the Public Concession and the French Concession have consulted and formulated the following methods for issuing travel car permits and driver's licenses: (1) Any car owner who holds a driver's license and car permit issued by a relevant local government authority and who resides outside the Shanghai Municipality, the Shanghai French Concession, and the Public Concession may obtain a special driver's license and a temporary vehicle permit for use within the two Shanghai concessions. The maximum validity period is 30 days. (2) Before entering the Shanghai Concessions, the car owner must first obtain a special pass from the China Automobile Association or the police department of the two concessions. One part of this pass, stating the type of car, must be affixed to the front windshield before entering the Concessions to complete the registration procedures. However, if they arrive at the Concession after business hours, they must complete the registration promptly at the beginning of business hours the next morning. Their car may be temporarily allowed to pass. (3) After the car owner presents the special pass, the concession authorities must inspect the car body and test the driver before issuing the vehicle and driver's licenses. (4) The validity period of the temporary driver's license and car permit must not exceed 20 days, after which it will be considered invalid. (5) When obtaining the license, the car owner must pay a security deposit of 30 yuan in national currency. The car permit fee is 2 yuan in national currency for the first three days and 1 yuan in national currency for every three days (or less than three days) thereafter. The permit fee may be deducted from the security deposit, and the remaining balance will be refunded upon return of the license plate. (6) Drivers must comply with all current traffic regulations in the Concession, as well as the provisions for issuing driver's licenses and car permits, etc. (7) In the event of any violation, the car owner and driver shall be subject to appropriate penalties by the relevant authorities, and the court within the French Concession may impose a fine of 1 to 50 yuan. The license plates and official documents for the travel vehicles mentioned above have been prepared by the concession authorities, and their forms have also been submitted to the various police stations for record keeping. The special passbooks have also been handed over to the China Automobile Association for issuance. However, people who are not members of the association may also obtain the aforementioned travel permit.

Attending Representatives

Promotion Schedule

Landlord Interference

The association rented vacant land at the intersection of North Sichuan Road and Keneng Road to hold the Shanghai North District National Products Exhibition. The exhibition had been running for nearly a week when, yesterday, the landlord suddenly interfered, demanding demolition and vacating the premises. The association believes that promoting national products is a matter of national economy and people's livelihoods and has specifically scheduled an emergency board meeting at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce at 3 p.m. today to discuss countermeasures.

Joint Insurance Notary Office Adds Insurance Consultant 153

To resolve insurance waste and difficulties for all sectors, accountant Pan Xulun and Wang Haifan, among others, of this city, previously, in light of the increasingly developed domestic fire insurance business and the increasing number of loss compensation events, and with public notarization as a profession, serving various insurance companies and policyholders, Chinese people, there were few who had seen them. Specialists gathered to establish the Joint Insurance Notary Office, which was approved by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for record-keeping, to perform the duties of a notary. Since starting their practice, accumulating experience based on facts, they deeply understand that Chinese people lack sophisticated research on insurance matters. Due to not understanding insurance regulations, or neglecting prior considerations, or not understanding the conditions to be observed during the effective period of the contract, or not knowing the proper steps to take after an accident, the reason is that both the usual waste of excessive premiums, increasing unnecessary burdens, and in case of damage, not being able to obtain appropriate compensation, resulting in a majority of serious and difficult recoveries. Therefore, recently, based on the original intention of serving society, in order to alleviate the above-mentioned pain and waste for all sectors, a method of adding a permanent insurance consultant has been specially added to prepare for the consultation of those who need insurance, to plan for them, so that the premiums will not be wasted, and in the future, in case of accidents, there will be no need to suffer heavy losses despite having insurance. It is said that this kind of service organization is still the first in the country, and its fees are extremely low, and in the future, it will benefit China's insurance industry, which should not be small.

Case of the Assassination of Tang Jiapeng - The Police Appeal Wang Xinggao - The Court Orders Wang to Provide an Additional 10,000 Yuan Guarantee 157

In the case of the assassination of Tang Jiapeng, the suspect Wang Xinggao, who was sentenced to life imprisonment, was declared innocent by the Third Branch of the High Court after appealing. During the appeal period, he was allowed to post a 10,000 yuan surety to leave. The Police Department, dissatisfied with the appeal judgment, requested the prosecutor of the Third Branch of the High Court to file an appeal with the Supreme Court. The High Court ruled that the appeal was approved. Yesterday morning, the Third Branch of the High Court summoned the appellant Wang Xinggao to court. At 12:30 p.m., Criminal Court President Zhu Huan _, accompanied by judges Wang and Liao, together with the chief prosecutor, arrived at the Criminal Court 5. Wang was summoned to the front of the case and briefly questioned about his age and origin. Then, two copies of the appeal were served to Wang Xinggao in court. It was announced that after the court declared you innocent in the murder case, you applied to suspend detention during the appeal period and were allowed to post a 10,000 yuan surety. Now that the appeal period has passed, the Police Department and the court prosecutor have filed an appeal. The case is in the appeal process, and you should find another 10,000 yuan guarantee to ensure that you will be available whenever summoned during the appeal and that you will not leave Shanghai during this period. If you cannot provide a guarantee, you will still be detained. Wang nodded in agreement and quickly said that he had a guarantor, saying, "Before the case is over, I will not look for trouble or leave Shanghai. I will be at home every day. I will come to court whenever the court summons me." The court verified the confession and ordered the bailiff to take the belt down and temporarily detain him, waiting for a guarantor. Wang's family also arrived at the court. Upon hearing the order, they went out to handle the procedures for finding a guarantor.

Wang Qiyuan's Frame-Up Case Involving Red Pills - Harming Others Hurts Themselves 159

Shishan native Wang Qiyuan (also known as Wang Zhongyin) once worked as an apprentice and accountant at the Tongtai North Goods Store jointly opened by Ye Fubao (also known as Hu Xiaozhou) and his father Wang Taosheng. He was later dismissed for embezzlement and ordered to return the embezzled funds, which led to resentment and a long-planned revenge. In early March of this year (lunar calendar), Wang Qiyuan came to Shanghai and stayed at the Yangtze River Hotel, where he met Zhang Hancheng (also known as Zhang Ahu), a fellow villager who worked as a tea boy at the hotel. He discussed a plan to buy red pills and frame someone. In early March (leap month), Zhang Hancheng went to Wang Qiyuan's Shanghai residence at No. 5 Zhongde Lane, Qinglian Street, and Wang Qiyuan gave him 52 yuan, instructing him to buy 8,000 red pills (8 packets of 1,000 pills each) from Yang Datou, who sold red pills, according to the previously agreed plan. He then returned to No. 5 Zhongde Lane and handed them over to Wang Qiyuan. Wang immediately took the red pills back to his home in Dingjiaqiao, Baoshan, and hid them in the spare room rented to Yang Wenbing, secretly planning to implement the frame-up. On one hand, he claimed that there were red pill wholesale agencies in Baoshan, Shanghai, and other places. He asked Chen Bin, whom Zhang Hancheng knew (Chen Bin was a former inspector of the Municipal Public Security Bureau's water patrol team and is now unemployed), to introduce him to Song Faxiang, and Yang Wenbing to be the accuser, issuing a written report. Chen Bin was the introducer, and Wang Qiyuan was the scribe. They waited to find out the location where the red pills were hidden before notifying them to report to Faixiang to report the crime. Later, according to Song Faxiang, there were red pill wholesale agencies near Shanghai, etc. When reporting to the Songhu Garrison Command, Wang Qiyuan learned that Ye Fubao's Shanghai residence, No. 148 Shangwen Road, Ximen, had a doctor, Wang Jianxiong, who rented the downstairs wing room as a medical room. On the afternoon of May 19, Wang Qiyuan took 3,000 red pills and led Zhang Hancheng and Yang Wenbing to Ye's house. Temporarily, Zhang Hancheng pretended to be sick and went to seek treatment. When Wang Qiyuan arrived at the gate of Ye's house, he handed 3,000 red pills to Yang Wenbing to enter, while Wang left on his own. At that time, there was only the nurse Tao Xingzhen in the medical room. While talking to the nurse, Yang Wenbing and Zhang Hancheng took the opportunity to throw 3,000 red pills handed over by Wang Qiyuan into the wooden plaque of the living room and escaped. Then, Chen Bin, together with Yang Wenbing, went to Song Faxiang to inform him that the red pill agency had been found. Song Faxiang reported to the Command Investigation Team by telephone. The Command sent investigators to supervise Song Faxiang, Yang Wenbing, and Ren Songlin, who was temporarily instructed by Song Faxiang to guard Yang Wenbing's eyeliner. They went to Ye Fubao's house to search and seized 3,000 red pills planted in the wooden plaque in the living room. The investigation team suspected something else and immediately took Song Faxiang, Chen Bin, Yang Wenbing, Ren Songlin, together with Ye Fubao's daughter-in-law Ye Baoshi (Hu Baoshi), and maid Zhuang Huibao, and other witnesses, to the team to interrogate. According to Yang Wenbing's confession, the truth was told. He said that the red pills were handed over and thrown in by Wang Qiyuan and Zhang Hancheng. There were still 5,000 red pills left in the original place in the countryside of Baoshan. Later, they went to Yang's house in Dingjiaqiao, Baoshan, and recovered the remaining 5,000 red pills from the planting. Zhang Hancheng and Wang Qiyuan were detained and sent to the team. According to Wang Qiyuan's confession, the circumstances of the frame-up were clear. Zhang Hancheng also confessed to the process of buying the pills and planting them. The team first allowed the victims Hu Baoshi and others to be released on bail and sent Song Faxiang and others, together with the 8,000 red pills seized, to the Command for handling. After detailed interrogation by the Military Law Department of the Command, they were sentenced to Wang Qiyuan (Wang Zhongyin), Zhang Hancheng (Zhang Ahu), and Yang Wenbing for jointly framing others with red pills for selling. Wang Qiyuan was sentenced to 15 years of fixed-term imprisonment and deprived of civil rights for ten years. Zhang Hancheng and Yang Wenbing were each sentenced to 12 years of fixed-term imprisonment and deprived of civil rights for ten years. Harming others harmed themselves under the law. This can be used as a warning for those who intend to frame others.

Case of the Assassination of Tang Youren - Continued Trial of Suspects - The Police Request a Postponement Because the Investigation Procedures Have Not Been Completed - All Defendants Unanimously Deny Participation in the Assassination 160

Former Minister of Foreign Affairs Tang Youren, a native of Hunan, was assassinated in front of his residence on Gansidong Road in the French Concession on the evening of December 25 last year. The French Police Department issued a general order to arrest the murderer, but to no avail. Recently, the Public Police Department arrested six robbers, Wang Guifu, Peng Renjie, Zhang Shilin, Yuan Youqiao, Gu Xiaohu, and Qiu Jiyu, last month. A pistol was seized. After the gun examination office verified that the gun was the same as the murder weapon in the Tang case, the case was reported to the First Special Court, which sentenced them to the crime of robbery. The French Police Department was notified and detectives were sent to bring the bandits back. On the 4th of this month, they were escorted to the Second Special Court for interrogation and detention. All details have been recorded in this newspaper. Yesterday was the date for the continued trial. At 9 a.m., Criminal Court President Wang Wangxu, accompanied by clerk Gao Yanmao, came to Criminal Court 1 to continue the trial. Defendant Peng Renjie was seriously ill with syphilis in detention and was sent to the hospital for treatment. He was unable to appear in court. Fei Xizhen, a lawyer from the Police Department, claimed to the court that the case was important and extremely complicated, so the investigation procedures had not been completed. The main criminal, Xiao Hangzhou, had fled to Hankou, and the detectives sent to arrest him had not returned. He requested that the detention period be extended for another two weeks. Defendant Qiu Jiyu stated that when Tang Youren was killed, he was in Hangzhou. The police are investigating, but it is not true. He was in Hangzhou in February of this year. He asked the court to pay attention to this point. The court ordered Detective Shi Qing, who was handling the case, to be brought to court to report on the investigation. Shi said that the detectives who arrested the fugitive Xiao Hangzhou had not yet returned to Shanghai. The police must strictly investigate this case. The court then questioned the four defendants, Wang Duifu, Zhang Shilin, Yuan Youqiao, and Gu Xiaohu. They said that they were all in their hometowns on December 25 of last year and knew nothing about the Tang Youren assassination. The robbery case was also a wrongful arrest. Qiu Jiyu confessed to participating in the Xiaoshadu Road robbery. The pistol was given to him by the fugitive Xiao Hangzhou during the robbery. He did not know where the gun came from. He knew nothing about the killing of Tang Youren. The defendants also claimed to the court that the treatment in the police station was poor and requested to be transferred to the detention center. They requested permission to file an appeal against the sentence of imprisonment for robbery by the First Special Court, otherwise the appeal period would be delayed. After verifying the confessions, the court ordered that the case be postponed to the 31st for another trial. The defendants were still returned to the police station, and the detectives handling the case were instructed to obtain confessions from the defendants using proper procedures and to assist them in filing appeals. After the instructions, the court adjourned.

Apprentice Injured and Dies in Swing Accident During Night School, Forensic Examination Concludes Death Due to Accidental Fall 168

The Yu Li Printing House, located at 291 Rue Joffre in the French Concession, is owned by Wu Rongfang from Anhui. The business is quite prosperous, and Mr. Wu also places great emphasis on the education of his workers and apprentices. After the work in the shop is finished, he sends them to Hua Guang Elementary School at 299 Rue Pere Robert to attend night classes and increase their knowledge. However, on the 15th of this month, at around 6 PM, an apprentice named Yan Shanfeng (from Ningbo, 16 years old) went to the school with his companions Gu Xiaodi and Peng Songquan. Seeing that the class time had not yet arrived, Yan and the others played on the swings in the school playground. Unexpectedly, Yan was careless and fell, sustaining serious injuries. He was taken to Guangci Hospital for treatment, where the doctors determined that Yan's injuries were internal and required surgery, which Yan refused. He returned to Yu Li Printing House and sought medical treatment, but it was ineffective. Mr. Wu then sent Yan to Xianglin Hospital at 578 Beijing Road for emergency treatment, but it was to no avail. He died the day before yesterday. The hospital reported the death to the Lao Zha Police Station, who sent detectives to investigate. The body was then transported to the Fei Lun Road morgue. Yesterday morning, Zhang Zongru, a prosecutor from the First Special District Court, along with forensic doctor Zhang Yan and a clerk, arrived at the morgue to examine the body. The examination confirmed that the deceased, Yan Shanfeng, was male and had died from injuries sustained in an accidental fall. The body was handed over to his uncle, Jiang Ziqing, for burial after he signed the necessary documents.
