Gang Arrested at Dafang Hotel, Investigation Reveals Plot to Rob Morphine, Two Unrelated Persons Released, Case Concluded and Scheduled for Sentencing on the 23rd 173

On the morning of the 1st of this month at around 2 AM, Inspector Jiang Futian of the French Police received a tip from an informant that a gang was hiding in room 204 on the second floor of the Dafang Hotel at No. 33 Zhengjia Muqiao. He immediately led the officers on duty to the address and arrested suspects Jin Baofa (35 years old, local, residing at No. 17 Hengmao Lane, Baxianqiao), Guo Yunyou (36 years old, from Hebei, residing upstairs at the Baohua Auto Repair Shop on Wuma Road), Chang Yaoting (29 years old, from Yangzhou, residing at No. 74 Zilaihuo Street), a woman, Xun Wangshi (28 years old, actress, residing at No. 8 Baokang Lane, Beijing Road), Chen Tingsheng (34 years old, from Zhenjiang, residing at No. 26 Yangjia Lane, Julai Road), and confiscated two handguns and 28 bullets. They were escorted to the Second Special District Court for interrogation and detention. This was reported in your newspaper. After investigation, the police found that Dong Wangshi and Chen Tingsheng were not involved and requested the court to release them first. The Police Department prosecuted the three defendants, Jin, Guo, and Chang, for the crime of possessing military firearms with intent to commit a crime under Article 187 of the Criminal Law, and the crime of robbery under Article 328, paragraph 5 of the same law. Yesterday morning at 8 AM, Judge Wang Gangxu presided over the trial in the Criminal Division No. 1. The court first summoned Chen Hanquan and Shen Peichun, tea servers at the Dafang Hotel, as witnesses. They testified that a Mr. Wu came to open room 204 on the afternoon of the 30th of last month. Late at night, three men and a young woman came together and were then arrested. Next, Inspector Jiang Futian of the Police Department, who handled the case, was summoned to the stand and questioned about the process of solving the case. Jiang testified that the defendants had confessed to planning to rob morphine near Zhonghua Lane. Finally, the court questioned the defendant Jin Baofa, who testified that he and Dong Wangshi were playing on the street that night when they met Chang Fukang, who was on the run, and were invited to the Dafang Hotel for a chat and some snacks. They went together. When they arrived in the room, Chang Fukang said his feet itched and took off his socks to take a bath. After he left the room, they were arrested. He did not know there were handguns in the room. He confessed in the police station because he was forced to confess by being doused with tap water and beaten with iron rods. He had never suffered such pain in his thirty-five years of life. Chang Fukang never returned and left a short Xiangyun gauze shirt in the room. Guo Yunyou and Chang Yaoting both testified that they denied the crime of plotting robbery and were framed. After the Police Department's lawyer and the defendants' lawyer Tang Hao debated, the court adjourned and scheduled the sentencing for the morning of the 23rd. The defendants were transferred back to the detention center.

Report on Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Changes in the First Quarter of This Year Edited by Zhu Zheng (30th Overview of Shanghai Industry and Commerce) 174

The following is a list of various changes in Shanghai's industry and commerce in the first three months of this year, with a particular emphasis on noteworthy businesses, listed by month for reference by all sectors of society.

(1) For January The new British-owned Meihua Bank began operations on the 15th of this month, but the official opening date has not yet been announced. The bank was formed by merging with the former Daxin Industrial Bank, which had been operating at 210 Sichuan Road for many years, so it seems more appropriate to list it as an expansion. In the money exchange industry, two companies expanded their capital, two companies reduced their capital, eight companies reorganized, and four companies closed down during this month, according to the Money Exchange Association. The general decline of the money exchange industry last year is noteworthy. In the transportation industry, the Chinese-owned Lili Automobile Company suddenly announced its closure on the 14th. The company was large-scale, with 80 cars, and was known as a leader in the industry. Its impact on the car rental industry was as great as that of the Public Yellow Automobile Company, which closed down in October last year. The reorganization and resumption of operations of the Zhonghua Ming Match Factory in the chemical industry is also noteworthy. The company had been closed for more than a year since it announced its closure at the same time as the Taifeng Canned Food Company in December 1934. In the woolen and foreign goods sales industry, one company contracted and ten companies reorganized this month. This is a large difference compared to the one company that reorganized in November last year, the lack of any reorganization or closure in December, and the one company that reorganized in the same period last year. In addition, the wool and cold storage industry also had considerable changes. In the midst of a trade surplus, it seems that it should not be ignored. The Daxin Co., Ltd., which had been preparing for a long time, announced its opening on the 10th of this month. The company has a total capital of 6 million Hong Kong dollars and its head office is located in Hong Kong. This is a major development in the city's department store industry.

(2) For February The American Express Bank announced the cessation of its banking business in the middle of this month. The bank was the Shanghai branch of the American head office and had been in operation for more than nineteen years. The cessation of banking business is said to be a planned move by the bank to prepare for the expansion of its transportation, travel and other businesses. Baochang Money Exchange is a member of the city's Money Exchange Association, with a capital of 140,000 yuan and a supplementary capital of 140,000 yuan. Its business was generally stable. However, due to the economic downturn and the lack of certainty about the future of the business, the shareholders voluntarily announced the closure. Two more gold shops closed down this month. Since the currency reform last year, nine companies have closed down one after another since April: Jiatai, Yuankangxiang, and Xie Daxiang at the end of October; Juchangyuan, Yongyi, and Fengdiyong in November; Ren Cheng in December; and Sheng Dayongji and Yuandayong in this month.

(3) For March A. In the financial industry: (1) The Central Savings Association officially announced its opening on the 16th. The association was established with funds allocated by the Central Trust Bureau, with a capital of 5 million yuan, and appointed Mr. Li Shuming as the manager. It specializes in prize savings. All depositors of the former Sino-French Savings Association were taken over by the association. (2) The Bank Acceptance House was also established on the 16th. The House was established by the Shanghai Banking Association and based on the resolution of the Shanghai Joint Reserve Committee's Bank Representatives Congress. It specializes in acceptance business between colleagues in the industry. The manager is Mr. Zhu Boquan. 38 banks have joined, and the acceptance fund is 7,623,750 yuan. This is a new development in the cooperation between banks. B. In public utilities: The Pudong Electric Company decided at its annual shareholders' meeting to increase its capital by another 500,000 yuan. The International Telecommunications Bureau was abolished by order of the Ministry of Communications. These are the two major changes in the city's public utilities. C. In the industrial sector: (1) The Guangdong Brothers Rubber Company announced its closure in mid-December last year due to the impact of the sharp drop in prices. In recent months, due to excessive debt, it has been unable to resume operations. This time, the creditors decided to jointly maintain the resumption of operations and formed a maintenance business committee to manage production. The company's head office is located in Hong Kong, and the Shanghai branch was founded in 1927. It employs more than 360 workers and can produce 10,000 dozen rubber shoes per day. The impact on the rubber industry is significant. (2) The closure of the Yangzi Flour Company is also a loss to the flour industry. Although the company's factory is located in Xiaguan, Nanjing, it has a general office in Shanghai. The capital is 300,000 yuan, and the maximum daily flour production is 10,000 bags. D. In the sales industry, in addition to the aforementioned new department stores, the establishment of two joint sales offices this month is also noteworthy: one is the opening of the China Machine-made Stone Powder Joint Sales Office, and the other is the establishment of the Xing'an Sugarcane Sales Office. The China Machine-made Stone Powder Joint Sales Office is jointly established by the Shanghai members of the China Machine-made Stone Powder Factory Association, Shunchang, Ruitai, Zhenxin, China, and the Wuxi members Chengtai, Chengda, Yongli, and other machine-made stone powder factories for the purpose of selling the products of each factory. The Xing'an Sugarcane Sales Office is composed of 16 sugar merchants, Zhicheng, Jichun, Fanglai, Jiechun, Fuyu, Tianxiang, Heshen, Defeng, Zhenxing, Wanhe, Zhaotai, Tongchang, Sanchun, Wanchun, Fucheng, and Taiyuan, for the purpose of promoting Fujian sugarcane. In recent years, the trend of production and sales cooperation in China's industry and commerce has become increasingly common, which is also a welcome phenomenon. (End)

In addition, the winners of the eight groups in the recent amateur boxing competition held in Chicago, USA, will all attend Berlin, including Louis Laurie, Jacques Wilson, Tito Tugarala, Sigfried Venn, Howard King, Jimmy Clark, Vincent Kuehler, and Oliver. The losers in the competition will be reserves.

Germany

German Olympic Committee Chairman Osten advocated that the number of athletes be set at 448, including 401 male athletes and 47 female athletes. They will participate in 19 events, including 67 in track and field, 25 in swimming, 30 in rowing, 28 in wrestling, and 22 in football, hockey, and handball. As for female athletes, there will be 18 in track and field and swimming each, 8 in indoor sports, and 3 in fencing. The list of athletes will be officially finalized in the middle of July, because Germany is currently busy entertaining guests and preparing for various Olympic Games in advance. However, Germany has the largest number of athletes participating in the conference.

Educational News

All Provinces and Cities to Double Fundraising for Compulsory Education Funds This Year; Ministry of Education Has Drafted Measures, Central Government to Discuss Immediately 189

The total amount of central government subsidies for education funds in various provinces and cities for the 25th year is 4.6 million yuan, an increase of 1.4 million yuan compared to the previous year (the central government subsidy for the previous year was 2.4 million yuan, plus 300,000 yuan for border education and 530,000 yuan, totaling 3.2 million yuan). This has been published in this newspaper. It is understood that the funds required for various provinces, cities, and districts to implement compulsory education are, except for remote provinces and impoverished provinces and regions that may receive special subsidies from the central government, based on Article 6 of the "Outline of Measures for Implementing Compulsory Education" promulgated and implemented by the central government, "The funding for compulsory education should be borne by the local governments in principle, but for remote, impoverished provinces and cities and other provinces and cities with special circumstances, the central government may provide appropriate subsidies." and Article 23 of the "Detailed Rules for the Implementation of the Outline of Measures for Implementing Compulsory Education", "The funding for compulsory education shall be unified by the government in urban areas, and in the counties and cities of the provinces, it shall be borne by the province and county in proportion. The central government may also subsidize the provinces and cities according to the circumstances." It is therefore the principle that each province and city should raise as much as possible on its own. Now that the central government has increased the subsidy for compulsory education funds for various provinces and cities by 1.4 million yuan compared to the previous year, in order to actively promote compulsory education and meet the urgent needs in reality, it is also required that each province and city raise its own funds for compulsory education, doubling the amount raised in the 24th year. The standards and methods for this increased fundraising by various provinces and cities in the 25th year have been drafted by the Ministry of Education and submitted to the Executive Yuan for review. It is said that the central government meeting will be held soon to approve and promulgate it.

(Nanjing, 27th) - Ding Weifen, President of the Central Political School of Education, visited Secretary-General Weng and Dean Wang on the 17th to discuss the establishment of an employment guidance class for college and university graduates. Li Jinxi Arrives in Beijing to Discuss Phonetic Chinese Characters; Beneficial for Preventing Cheating 191

Li Jinxi, Dean of the College of Liberal Arts at the National Peiping Normal University, arrived in Beijing at the end of last month from the north to broadcast "Phonetic Symbols and Simplified Characters" and to discuss official business with the Ministry of Education. According to reports, the progress, advantages, and disadvantages of promoting phonetic Chinese characters, and the suspension of simplified characters, are as follows:

Phonetic Chinese Characters Are Being Promoted

The government spent a huge amount of money to promote short-term compulsory education last year, and this year it has increased it to more than 4 million yuan. At the same time, it is promoting civil education, with more than one million yuan in funding. This type of education must be widespread and have practical effects. The key point is still the improvement of language tools. Phonetic Chinese characters are used to assist the public in literacy with the help of phonetic symbols. The purpose is not to unify the country. The Ministry of Education allocated 20,000 yuan last year to cast bronze molds of phonetic Chinese characters. Each set has four sizes: two, three, four, and five. Each set has more than 5,000 to 7,000 characters. It is stipulated that from July 1st of this year, all textbooks and supplementary reading materials for primary schools and civil schools must be printed with phonetic Chinese characters, otherwise they will not be approved or will be punished. According to a survey by the National Language Promotion Committee, these textbooks have been widely used in the past six months. However, there is a lack of teachers, which often makes the phonetic symbols next to the characters equivalent to double dumbness. Therefore, I came to Beijing this time to propose to the ministry based on the resolutions of the National Language Conference to focus on teachers, avoid perfunctory work, and seek simplification and universalization in the transmission of phonetic symbols. The bronze molds cast by the Ministry, sizes two and three, have been delivered by the Zhonghua Book Company, and sizes four and five will be completed soon. The Sai bronze molds cast by the Commercial Press have already produced phonetic size three characters, which are also beautiful and very cheap.

Phonetic Chinese Characters are Beneficial and Have No Drawbacks

People in the education field are concerned about the disadvantages of paying attention to Chinese characters: (1) Replacing characters with sounds is overwhelming. They do not know that Chinese characters are necessary for the living environment, and there is no one who only reads the phonetic symbols next to them. Those who already know how to read characters can focus on reading Chinese characters, regardless of the phonetic symbols on the right. If they encounter a new character, they can know the meaning from the sound by looking at the phonetic symbols. If they know very few characters, the right side is the "teacher," and they can learn characters from the sound. If they do not know any characters at all, they can understand the meaning by temporarily spelling out the sounds. Like this, the guest and host complement each other, so how can it be overwhelming? (2) Text printing is more troublesome. They do not know that the movable type of phonetic Chinese characters has the phonetic symbols fixed on the right side of the Chinese characters. With this printing tool, those who write the text do not have to add phonetic symbols, and they can be sent to print. Typesetters do not have to typeset phonetic symbols, which is a win-win situation. Proofreaders do not have to look at the phonetic symbols, and there will be no errors. After the book is completed, it is clear and beautiful. However, those who learn phonetic symbols can all read. (3) The size of the phonetic symbols harms eyesight. They do not know that all new reading materials for children and the public currently use size four Chinese characters, and no one uses size five. Textbooks use even larger characters, size two and above. The fixed phonetic symbols on the right are not small in shape, the strokes are simple, and they are a reference, not the main reading. How can it harm eyesight? (4) The printing is flashy and dazzling. This is because intellectuals who already know many characters do not realize it and criticize it casually. They have not thought about it for children and the illiterate public who are learning to read. It is not worth arguing. (5) Preparing but not using them results in redundancy. This should only focus on teachers and not throw the baby out with the bathwater. My coming here is to remedy this shortcoming.

Simplified Characters are Still Used Freely

The list of simplified characters was announced by the Ministry of Education in August of the Earth year (likely referring to a year in the Chinese sexagenary cycle). It contains 324 characters, most of which are already commonly used in society. Originally, they could have been implemented automatically without promotion. In January of this year, the Executive Yuan ordered "postponing implementation." Those who misunderstand this think that this is a prohibition on using simplified characters. They do not know that the Yuan order is to delay the nine articles of the "Measures for Promoting Simplified Characters Promulgated by the Ministry of Education by Educational Administrative Organs in Various Provinces and Cities," not to cancel the announced list of simplified characters. In the future, if textbooks and other materials want to use simplified characters, they can still use them freely. Junior high schools are all subject to review and approval, and the general public can still write simplified characters. Who will interfere? The announcement of the list of simplified characters is only to indicate "review completed" and "recognition." In addition to this first batch, a full spectrum should be created for use in primary schools and civil schools to learn to write characters. Because simplified characters are only for convenient writing and have nothing to do with reading, while phonetic Chinese characters are only for convenient reading and have nothing to do with writing. It is said that Mr. Li will take a ship to Hunan as soon as he finishes his official business with the Ministry of Education.

Modification Points of the Teacher Training Curriculum Standards; Elementary Teacher and Rural Teacher and Kindergarten Teacher 195

The National Compilation and Translation Bureau previously presented to the Ministry of Education, stating that several sections in the current curriculum standards for elementary normal schools and elementary rural normal schools should be slightly modified: (1) Civic Moral Life, (1) (10) "Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Psychological Construction Theory" should be moved back and changed to Civic Political Life, (3) (4) because it is the basic condition for revolutionary construction. (2) Civic Moral Life (3) (3) In "The National Intrinsic Advantages and Research," the words "and Research" should be deleted, because the existence of these three characters is not only meaningless but also confusing. (3) General Principles of Law, (2) Under "Subject and Object of Rights," there were originally three sections: one is the meaning of rights, the second is the types of rights, and the third is natural persons and legal persons. According to the "natural persons and legal persons" are the subjects of rights, which has been listed as a detail, the object of rights should also be listed as a detail. It is proposed to change it as follows: (2) Subject and Object of Rights, (1) The meaning and types of rights, (2) Natural persons and legal persons, (3) Things, (4) Civic Economic Life, (5) Under "Distribution," there were originally four sections, but the item of land rent is missing. It is proposed to add the three characters "Land Rent and" to "Wages." In addition, the law of the civic curriculum standard for the two-year kindergarten teacher training course, (4) the section on "Ownership of Real Estate" should be deleted, because the section on ownership before it did not specify that it only talked about movable property. Recently, the Ministry of Education issued an instruction that the above-mentioned sections should be approved for modification.

Schools Should Refund Fees Collected from Students That Should Be Refunded; Municipal Education Bureau Strictly Orders Schools to Comply 196

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued an order yesterday to public and private primary and secondary schools, stating that it has been ordered by the Bureau's No. 4493 order that students should not be charged extra graduation fees upon graduation. Now it is found that when new students enroll, some schools collect security deposits, and some collect compensation for damage fees. When students graduate, the security deposits that should be refunded are not refunded. Students have not damaged school property, and the compensation for damage fees collected is also not refunded, which is very inappropriate. In addition to sending staff to investigate separately, fees that should be refunded to students in the future must be refunded in full. Otherwise, they will be severely punished. All schools must comply with this order.

Jiangsu Education Department Orders the Holding of Summer Vacation Training for Elementary School Teachers 203

July 20th to August 16th (Zhenjiang News) - The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education has previously ordered the holding of summer vacation training meetings for elementary school teachers in various districts, according to the order of the Ministry of Education. The Ministry of Education has determined the methods and submitted them for approval. Now, the Ministry of Education has stipulated that the training period for this year will still be four weeks (from July 22nd to August 16th). The training subjects in each district are uniformly "Single-Grade Teaching Method," "Knowledge Teaching Materials and Teaching Methods," "Model Teaching and Practice," "Phonetic Symbols," and "Abacus," etc., and can appropriately add subjects such as practical problems in primary schools. The school is currently recruiting new Chinese and foreign male and female students and has added a junior class to provide more opportunities for beginners, as well as a summer class for remedial studies.

申報婦女專刊

Shen Bao Women's Supplement

一封喚起我們要求眞平等的信 236

A Letter Arousing Us to Demand True Equality 237

— 顧文淑

— Gu Wenshu

自從馳明的盧梭，發明了人類是一概平等的話；便引起了世界上莫大的騷動；好像帝制的被打倒，和民主的勃興等，但是除了這些外，還有一件也是被這學說所推動而發生的事，就是十九世紀以來的女權運動，全世界的婦女都在走上或預備走上解放的道路，希望不論在政治上，社會上，經濟上，要和男子受同等待遇，不過假使我們用顯微鏡的目光細察起來，我們就可以威覺到目前世界上，不論那一個女權最發達的國家，他國裏的婦女，還可以說沒有達到眞正的平等，那麼什麼纔是眞正的平等呢？下面一封信，可以指示我們眞正平等的方向，這封信是一個法國女子（Madame　Sante）寫給巴黎晚報（Paris—Soir）的，我現在把這對信翻在下面，貢獻給讀者們。

Since the renowned Rousseau invented the idea that all human beings are equal, it has caused great turmoil in the world, such as the overthrow of the imperial system and the rise of democracy. But besides these, there is another thing that has been promoted by this theory, that is, the feminist movement since the nineteenth century. Women all over the world are embarking on or preparing to embark on the road to liberation, hoping to receive the same treatment as men in politics, society, and economy. However, if we examine it carefully with a microscopic eye, we can feel that in the current world, no matter which country has the most developed women's rights, the women in that country can still be said to have not achieved true equality. So what is true equality? The following letter can point us in the direction of true equality. This letter was written by a French woman (Madame Sante) to the Paris evening newspaper (Paris—Soir). I will now translate this pair of letters below and contribute them to readers.

前天早晨，我（Sante自稱）出去買些雜物，因為我是個平常的主婦，在路上有一張佈告，吸引我的注意力。

The day before yesterday morning, I (Sante said myself) went out to buy some groceries, because I am an ordinary housewife, and on the road there was a notice that attracted my attention.

今日國家婦女連合會，開會討論反對戰爭與法西斯。

Today, the National Women's Federation will hold a meeting to discuss opposition to war and fascism.

我看了後，認為很不錯，我們女人不能讓男子們去胡作非為，我們也要出主意；我們須要不論在社會上，經濟上，政治上，宗教上，和他們平等，我們須要享有工作不受限制的權利，和男子同等的薪金，完全的選舉權和被選舉權等，後來我轉念一想，我們單是和男子爭和自己有利的權利，而對於和自己無利的權利像服兵等苦役，置之不聞不問，我想這種片面的，不完整的平等，決定不是天賦我（第二十六期）們的平等吧！

After reading it, I thought it was very good. We women cannot let men act recklessly. We must also come up with ideas. We must be equal to them in society, economy, politics, and religion. We must have the right to work without restrictions, the same salary as men, full voting rights and the right to be elected, etc. Later, I changed my mind and thought that we are only fighting with men for rights that are beneficial to ourselves, but for rights that are not beneficial to ourselves, such as military service and other hard labor, we turn a blind eye. I think this kind of one-sided, incomplete equality is definitely not the equality that God has given us (issue 26)!

全國的女同胞們，看了這封信，我們應當明白怎樣去找這神聖的眞平等了。

Female compatriots across the country, after reading this letter, we should understand how to find this sacred true equality.

蘇聯婚姻法的新改革 238

New Reforms in Soviet Marriage Law 239

— 魯沙白女士

— Ms. Lusha Bai

蘇聯的婚姻法原來是根據自由結婚法草成的，一面祗要男女兩性合意，便可以結婚，不受任何束縛。兩人中有一人要離婚，也祗須依法請求完成一個極簡單的手續，就可仳離。這是蘇聯自由結婚的根本精神，一向很受對蘇聯表示好感的各國的稱讚。但實際上運用起來，却不免有很多人利用離婚手續的簡單，使蘇聯的性道德陷於墮落。譬如家庭的破裂和兒童的棄置等事，隨處都可看見，這對於趨向社會主義建設的蘇聯社會，確是一大缺點。

The Soviet marriage law was originally drafted based on the Free Marriage Law. As long as both men and women agree, they can get married without any restrictions. If one of the two wants a divorce, they only need to apply in accordance with the law and complete a very simple procedure to divorce. This is the fundamental spirit of Soviet free marriage, which has always been praised by countries that express goodwill towards the Soviet Union. However, in practice, many people inevitably take advantage of the simplicity of the divorce procedures to make Soviet sexual morality fall into depravity. For example, the breakdown of families and the abandonment of children can be seen everywhere. This is indeed a major shortcoming for Soviet society, which is moving towards socialist construction.

蘇聯當局對這事實，極為重視，便積極進行改革結婚法；今年五月二十六日，便將改革的方案，交各官廳，工塲，農塲上作普遍的討論，微求大衆的意見。這次結婚法改革的內容相當廣泛，它的根本原則仍是以自由結婚法為基礎，但特別重視父母的義務，同時更注重家庭的意義。

The Soviet authorities attach great importance to this fact and actively carry out reforms in the marriage law. On May 26 of this year, the reform plan was submitted to government offices, factories, and farms for general discussion, seeking the opinions of the public. The content of this marriage law reform is quite extensive. Its fundamental principle is still based on the Free Marriage Law, but it pays special attention to the obligations of parents and at the same time pays more attention to the meaning of family.

改革後的婚姻法，第一是離婚較前困難；從來離婚登記費要繳五盧布，現在增加為第一次離婚繳五十盧布，第二次離婚繳一百五十盧布，第三次離婚繳三百盧布。離婚時倘有子女，應歸母親扶養，但由父親支出月薪的三分之一供給母親作兒童的撫養費，倘不履行道條約，卽判處兩年的徒刑。

The first reform of the marriage law is that divorce is more difficult than before. In the past, the divorce registration fee was five rubles, but now it has been increased to fifty rubles for the first divorce, one hundred and fifty rubles for the second divorce, and three hundred rubles for the third divorce. If there are children at the time of divorce, they should be raised by the mother, but the father should pay one-third of his monthly salary to the mother as child support. If the treaty is not fulfilled, he will be sentenced to two years in prison.

男子負有支付撫養費的義務時，他的護照上卽有詳細的記載，無論他在蘇聯邦任何地方工作，都經常由月薪中扣除，不得拖欠。至於離婚的手續，也仍只要一方的意志卽可成立，離婚通知書也只須用掛號寄去卽可。這仍舊保存昔日自由結婚的精神，但不過加重了離婚前後的經濟負担，對那般隨意離合的男女加以限制而巳。

When a man has the obligation to pay child support, his passport will have detailed records. No matter where he works in the Soviet Union, it will be regularly deducted from his monthly salary and cannot be in arrears. As for the divorce procedures, it can still be established as long as one party wills it, and the divorce notice only needs to be sent by registered mail. This still preserves the spirit of free marriage in the past, but it only increases the economic burden before and after divorce, and restricts those men and women who divorce at will.

據這次的改革看來，似乎特別限制男子，但對女子方面也有相當的限制。有子女的母親應負擔撫育子女的責任，倘不履行這種義務，父親有提起告訴之權：：所以這决的改革並不偏於任何一方，而是專重雙方為父母的責任的。

According to this reform, it seems to particularly restrict men, but there are also considerable restrictions on women. Mothers with children should bear the responsibility of raising their children. If they do not fulfill this obligation, the father has the right to file a lawsuit. Therefore, this reform does not favor either party, but focuses on the responsibility of both parties as parents.

改革的第二點是獎勵生育，有七個子女的父母，生到第八個後，從第一年到第五年，每年由政府津貼二千盧布：生到十一個以後，第一年給以五千盧布，第二年以後到第四年，每年給以三千盧布。蘇聯的這種積極獎勵生育，正是因為它的產業建設發展，一切需要着新的勞力，同時為了建設新的社會文化生活，所以政府對於多產多育者不能不予以經濟上的援助。

The second point of the reform is to encourage childbirth. Parents with seven children will receive a government subsidy of 2,000 rubles per year from the first to the fifth year after the birth of the eighth child. After the birth of the eleventh child, they will receive 5,000 rubles in the first year and 3,000 rubles per year from the second to the fourth year. The Soviet Union's active encouragement of childbirth is precisely because its industrial construction is developing and everything requires new labor. At the same time, in order to build a new social and cultural life, the government has to provide economic assistance to those who have many children.

改革的第三點是對妊婦的保護，禁止各地工廠藉故將妊婦停職或拒絕收用，違者嚴重處罰。在以前的結婚法中，本來也有這條規定，但這次改革後，對於任婦的保護更為周密，而對於上述將妊婦停職或拒絕收用妊婦者處罰，也較前更為嚴峻。

The third point of the reform is the protection of pregnant women. It is forbidden for factories in various places to suspend or refuse to hire pregnant women on the grounds of excuse. Violators will be severely punished. This provision was originally included in the previous marriage law, but after this reform, the protection of pregnant women is more comprehensive, and the penalties for suspending or refusing to hire pregnant women are more severe than before.

最後是關於墮胎問題，在革命後的混亂期間，因為男女都從事於社會工作，對於限制生育以至墮胎等，在那時只要當事人願意，卽可隨便實行。但因此也發生性道德的腐化，引起重大的社會缺憾。

Finally, there is the issue of abortion. During the chaos after the revolution, because both men and women were engaged in social work, limiting childbirth and even abortion could be carried out casually as long as the parties involved were willing. However, this also led to the corruption of sexual morality, causing major social regrets.

現在蘇聯的國民生活，巳趨安定，像墮胎這非法的手段早巳沒有必要，所以這次修改結婚法，便禁止一切危害母親身體的非法生產；違此禁例，卽處一年到三年的徒刑。但經醫生認為有墮胎的必要時，則不在禁止之列。同時並指定墮胎的孕婦，須在有最優良設備的國立病院中施受手術。

Now that the national life of the Soviet Union has become stable, there is no longer any need for illegal measures such as abortion. Therefore, this revision of the marriage law prohibits all illegal births that endanger the mother's body. Violators will be sentenced to one to three years in prison. However, if a doctor believes that abortion is necessary, it is not prohibited. At the same time, it is specified that pregnant women undergoing abortion must undergo surgery in national hospitals with the best equipment.

蘇聯政府更注意到對產婦的保護，特別研究無痛分娩的方法，最近已發現一種極有效果的方法，正在努力於這方法的普及。

The Soviet government has paid more attention to the protection of mothers and has conducted special research on painless childbirth methods. Recently, a very effective method has been discovered and efforts are being made to popularize this method.

以上是這次改革結婚决的梗概，由此可知蘇聯現在已重視到以家庭為中心的社會生活，但這次不是僅僅重視家庭生活，提倡舊的道德，而完全是新社會建設發展下必然的要求。確實，蘇聯現在的社會文化生活已一年一年地提高，人民生活富裕，國家經濟充實，在這一切社會基礎的反映下，為社會生活細胞的家庭，當然也要求着有更新的更健全的更美滿的生活，這次結婚的改革，便完成是由於這樣的動機。這確是蘇戀人民生活上的一大改革！

The above is an outline of this reform marriage decision. From this, we can see that the Soviet Union now attaches importance to family-centered social life, but this time it is not just about emphasizing family life and promoting old morality, but a necessary requirement under the development of new social construction. Indeed, the social and cultural life of the Soviet Union is improving year by year, the people's life is prosperous, and the national economy is enriched. Under the reflection of all these social foundations, the family, which is the cell of social life, of course also demands a newer, healthier and more satisfying life. The reform of this marriage was completed due to such motives. This is indeed a major reform in the lives of the Soviet people!

擇夫標準 240

Standards for Choosing a Husband 241

— 諸滕曼蓉

— Zhu Teng Manrong

老實說，一個女子如非另有了原因而才實行獨身主義的，那麽，到了相當年齡，誰都要經過一個「結婚」的階段。「結婚」當然是一樁大事；但是，我曾看見過很多的人？把「結婚」看得很輕，簡直不當一回事；不過她們也有理由，她們說：「結婚了要是「好」，那末不生問題；要是不好，則譬如沒有結婚，儘可離婚。」哼這種話說得好寫意，須知現行法律雖可離婚，但金錢與精神，一定兩受其損；並且譬如和甲結婚了不久就離婚，但離婚了再和乙結婚，但不久文離婚。像這樣的結婚離婚，眞是視同兒戲，試問，像這樣的女子，還能嫁得到好的丈夫嗎？還能得到社會的同情嗎？

To be honest, if a woman does not practice celibacy for other reasons, then at a certain age, everyone has to go through a stage of "marriage." "Marriage" is certainly a major event; but I have seen many people? Take "marriage" very lightly, simply not taking it seriously; but they also have reasons, they say: "If marriage is "good," then there is no problem; if it is not good, then it is as if you are not married, you can divorce." Hmph, these words are said so freely. It should be known that although the current law allows divorce, money and spirit will definitely be damaged; and for example, if you marry A and divorce soon, but after divorce you marry B, but soon divorce again. Marriage and divorce like this is really regarded as child's play. May I ask, can a woman like this marry a good husband? Can you get social sympathy?

「那麽要怎樣才能嫁得到好的丈夫呢？」這是一個很易解答的問題，自然，第一不要把「結婚」看得輕易，我們應當長存一個結婚了不能離婚的思想，這樣一來，自然會把「結婚」看得鄭重，把「結婚」看得鄭重了，那麽就須注重「擇夫」注重了「擇夫」，自然就能嫁到好的丈夫了！

"So how can you marry a good husband?" This is a very easy question to answer. Naturally, the first thing is not to take "marriage" lightly. We should always have the idea that we cannot divorce after marriage. In this way, we will naturally take "marriage" seriously. If we take "marriage" seriously, then we must pay attention to "choosing a husband." If we pay attention to "choosing a husband," we will naturally be able to marry a good husband!

不過「擇夫」也須預先定一個標準，但是這標準也得有些分寸；譬如，一個村姑想嫁出洋的留學生，一個女工想嫁銀行的總理，這都是出乎情理之外而又絕對不能成事實的擇夫標準；並且卽使萬一成了事實後，我敢說，將來也决無好果！所以我們在未定標準之前，須自己想想我是一個怎樣地位的入，應該和怎樣一等人結婚，是最合宜而又最美滿，總之，既不能媽虎，又不能苛求，須要合乎情理之內的定一個擇夫標準。

However, "choosing a husband" must also have a standard set in advance, but this standard must also have some propriety; for example, a village girl wants to marry a student studying abroad, and a female worker wants to marry the president of a bank. These are all standards for choosing a husband that are beyond reason and absolutely cannot become a reality; and even if it does become a reality, I dare say that there will be no good results in the future! Therefore, before we set a standard, we must think about what kind of person I am and what kind of people I should marry. It is the most appropriate and perfect. In short, we must neither be perfunctory nor demand too much. We must set a standard for choosing a husband that is within reason.

說起了擇夫標準，我又想起了一件關於這問題的事情：

Speaking of standards for choosing a husband, I remembered something about this issue again:

在我家的附近，有一　雜貨店，店主有一個女兒，二八年華，秀色可餐，她父親因為店中人少，所以教她輟了學助理店務。因此店中生意大好，附近的一輩子浮滑少年，且和她取了個「雜貨西施」的綽號！

Near my house, there is a grocery store. The owner has a daughter who is sixteen years old. She is beautiful and appetizing. Her father, because there were few people in the store, asked her to drop out of school to assist in the store business. As a result, the store's business is very good. The slippery young men nearby gave her the nickname "Grocery Xishi"!

「雜貨西施」到了這樣的年齡，當然有很多的人來和她作伐，但是，橫不成，豎不就，說了很多人，都不稱她的心

"Grocery Xishi" has reached this age, of course, many people come to make matches for her, but, it doesn't work horizontally or vertically. Many people have been talked about, but none of them meet her heart.

隔了很久，她終於和人結婚了，據說，對方是一個很漂亮的西裝少年，原來她就早定了一個擇夫標準：「不是西裝少年決不結婚！」所以她在初見時就十二分地滿意，然而，她就因了這滿意而鑄成大錯！原來，這漂亮的西裝少年，是一個毫無學識的理髮匠，她事前單看了表面，並沒有細細地探聽他的職業與學識，到結了婚才知道他是理髮匠，但是大錯鑄成，悔已莫及！

After a long time, she finally married someone. It is said that the other party is a very handsome young man in a suit. It turns out that she had set a standard for choosing a husband long ago: "I will never marry if he is not a young man in a suit!" So she was very satisfied when she first met him, but she made a big mistake because of this satisfaction! It turns out that this handsome young man in a suit is an uneducated barber. She only looked at the surface beforehand and did not inquire about his occupation and knowledge in detail. She only found out that he was a barber after she got married, but the big mistake was made, and it was too late to regret it!

頭髮報國的日本婦女 242

Japanese Women Who Serve the Country with Their Hair 243

— 一髪

— Yi Fa

在自認為非常時期的日本，十一年度的總預算，已達到二十三億以上。內中用於擴充軍備的費用的，當然已經可觀了。但是日本的國民還是紛紛獻金報國，以為後盾。小學生曾集香烟錫紙，以購愛國號飛機。現在又有一部份的婦女，提倡頭髮報國。在國難時期的我國，既沒有强力國防的，又無充分的經濟，不知我國女性將以何種方法，報答祖國。

In Japan, which considers itself in a period of emergency, the total budget for the eleventh year has reached over 2.3 billion. Of course, the expenses used to expand armaments are already considerable. However, the Japanese people are still donating money to serve the country as a backing. Elementary school students have collected cigarette tin foil to purchase patriotic airplanes. Now, a part of women are advocating serving the country with their hair. In our country, which is in a period of national crisis, without strong national defense and without sufficient economy, I wonder what methods our women will use to repay their motherland.

當一個女子在每天梳頭的時候，總有幾根頭髮，隨着木梳落下。普通便丟在垃圾箱裏，付之一炬。神奈川縣厚木町女子靑年團’於去年年底開始向各村各町，喚起婦女，囑將梳下的頭髮保存起來，一個月中已積得三十二斤，為製假髮店購去。得洋二元五角，獻與橫須賀海軍鎮守府，為國防費。得前大角海相的感謝狀、今歲四月將擴大宣傳，徵收全國女子加入。蒐集的方法，先用印有說明語的紙袋，發給村中各住家。每天便由女子靑年團派人挨戶收集，並以空袋調換，這個方法是仿警察局在暑天收集蒼蠅的方法。日本婦女對此很表同情，並不以兒戲視之。

When a woman combs her hair every day, there are always a few hairs that fall with the wooden comb. Usually they are thrown in the trash can and burned. The Kanagawa Prefecture Atsugi Town Women's Youth Group' began to call on women in various villages and towns at the end of last year to save the hair that was combed off. In one month, they have accumulated 32 catties, which were purchased by wig shops. Get two yuan and five jiao, donate it to the Yokosuka Naval Base for national defense expenses. Received a letter of thanks from former Minister of the Navy, Admiral Osumi. In April of this year, publicity will be expanded and women across the country will be recruited to join. The collection method is to first use paper bags printed with explanatory words and distribute them to each household in the village. Every day, the Women's Youth Group sends people to collect them door-to-door and exchange them for empty bags. This method is based on the method used by the police station to collect flies in the summer. Japanese women express great sympathy for this and do not regard it as child's play.

據做假髮的人說，現在科學雖然昌明，但是用人工製造頭髮，尚未發明。從前假髮都是用於舞台上的。自從都會女子，盛行剪髮之後。當出嫁時候，需用髮髻而一時又留不起來，於是不得不利用假髮。此外藝妓的習慣，是必需有高大的髮髻。剪髮女子，做藝妓的時候，也用假髮。故近年以來，假髮的銷路大增，而來源却仍是很少。製造假髮的頭髮

Self-Narration of Wang Aimei, a Female Cannery Worker 244

— Ji Ping

Want to eat, first need money; without working, where would money come from? Not reading, not knowing characters, is like a blind person with open eyes; earning a living by labor is the most honorable person in the world.

In the past six months, this reporter has interviewed more than twenty women, and each special feature has been disclosed in this publication. It is gratifying to have received sympathy from readers, inspiring people endlessly! Among these twenty-odd people are female pioneers, academic experts, social leaders, and new virtuous wives and good mothers, all of whom are rare talents in the female community. Each speaks their aspirations, each exhausts their intentions, and all discussions must have unique insights. As for the main purpose of interviewing them: first, to hear famous sayings and honest opinions, instructing women on how to be modern women? Second, to commend everyone's career and improve the status of women; third, to give women an opportunity to express their opinions, to expand everyone's aspirations, aiming to improve family life and education, advocating equal rights for men and women, and advocating that women establish a spirit of impartiality and selflessness, and jointly contribute to the cause of society and the country. However, women's issues are multifaceted. In the future, in addition to the established policies, we will from time to time collect living materials of working women to seek a way out for women's liberation. Here, we will first introduce the life of a female cannery worker, which can also reveal her inner reflections.

(1)

The Kangyuan Cannery is recognized as a national goods factory with sound organization and successful implementation of scientific management. The day before yesterday, when I walked into the factory, hundreds of workers were working diligently. Among them was a female worker numbered 782. Her operation was indeed agile. I then invited her to the reception room for a normal conversation. Her name is Wang Aimei, a native of Jiangwan, Shanghai. She is only twenty-eight years old. Sadly, she has been a widow for two years! I first investigated her background and family situation. She said: "I grew up in Jiangwan, where my family has been farming for generations. I got married at the age of twenty-two. My husband was originally a foreman at the Kangyuan factory. After marriage, I also entered the factory to work. In the past six or seven years, we lived by our craftsmanship and were quite comfortable. Unfortunately, my husband passed away two years ago. The orphan is now only four years old and is being cared for by my loving mother. I remember that when my late husband was alive, we were very loving and never had disagreements. I wanted to build a family business, but who would have expected such a tragic change. I only lament my thin fate. I now live near the factory, and the monthly cost of food and lodging is twelve yuan, and the cost of clothing and miscellaneous items is five or six yuan. The monthly wage, including overtime and Sunday work, is twenty yuan, which is enough to maintain life. My husband's old mother is still alive. Because I have very little spare time, I cannot often serve her. After all, it is hard for poor people, and the body is not free. Earning money is not easy, and it is really difficult to do my filial piety. I guess rich people can always do their filial piety, right?"

(2)

The next question was about her work interest...colleague feelings and treatment in the factory. She thought for a while and said in an orderly manner: "I am in the packaging section of the canning department. I start work at 7 am every morning until 12 noon, and from 2 pm to 5:30 pm. I also work overtime for two or three hours. I work, eat, rest, and sleep like this day and night. When today is done, I do it again tomorrow. People are like machines. As for the joys and sorrows, I don't feel much. I want to eat, first I need money, and to get money, I must work. We are poor people, with no permanent property, relying on our own hands, working one day and eating one day. We are used to it and don't feel the hardship. I think only by being calm and relying on our own labor can we seek personal survival. Otherwise, how can the world be peaceful! There are more than a hundred female workers in this factory. We go in and out together every day, but the factory rules do not allow talking during work, so everyone is familiar but does not talk much. Every Saturday, a general meeting is held, bringing all 400 workers in the factory together to listen to the general manager's instructions. Besides that, there is little contact. My opinions on general female workers can be divided into two aspects: (1) Some are quick-eyed and quick-handed, and ship goods quickly; (2) Some pay attention to cleanliness and are strong; (3) Some are steady in their work and do not need to be managed by others. But there are few good people and many bad people. I most disapprove of things like (1) being lazy at work and not listening to others' advice; (2) not being determined to work and hindering others; (3) dirty clothes and weak health. The factory treats us very well. For example, if a female worker is pregnant, she first registers with the personnel department and goes to the designated hospital. The expenses are provided by the factory, and she gets one month of leave before and after childbirth, with full pay. This is also the case when she is sick. In all fairness, it can be considered preferential treatment."

(3)

Finally, she was asked how many years she had studied when she was a child... How can she be satisfied with her life? She expressed her sadness about these points: "I only blame my parents for spoiling me too much. What's the use of studying for more than a year? My hometown is more than ten miles away from the school, and it's too far to go back and forth. To this day, not being able to read books and newspapers is really like being blind with open eyes. Probably only two or three out of ten female workers are literate. If you don't study when you are young, you will suffer a lot when you are old. Speaking of my life, there is nothing I am not satisfied with. Earning a living by my own efforts is the freest and most honorable person in the world. I don't dream in vain either. I only hope to raise my son to be an adult, read more books, and study hard. With strong skills, he can do some outstanding work and never be like his mother, suffering here."

Standard Wife 245

— Man Ling Huang

My friend works in a factory. They have two children and an old nanny. His wife is extremely capable and can handle all the big and small things in the house herself. I will write down some of her work for the reference of female compatriots. Can you not consider me excessive for calling her "standard"?

Every day before six o'clock, when her husband and children are still sound asleep, she gets up quietly. At this time, she calls the old nanny to start the fire and cook porridge. On the one hand, she washes up herself first, and then helps the old nanny sweep the house. At seven o'clock, the two children get up, and she washes their faces and tidies up their books for them. On the one hand, she teaches them one by one how they should do things themselves. At the same time, she orders the old nanny to prepare porridge and vegetables for the children to eat. At eight o'clock, the old nanny sends the children to school. Her husband likes to sleep and does not get up until after eight fifteen. After the children and servants leave home, she prepares the things that her husband will use when he gets up, such as shirts, socks, handkerchiefs, etc., and puts them one by one on the side of the bed. The water for washing his face is ready next to the washbasin. While her husband is washing his face, she has already prepared breakfast. At eight thirty, her husband goes to work, and the old nanny comes back. Then she goes to the vegetable market. Before leaving, she always instructs the old nanny to wash the floor. Before eleven thirty, she helps to cut vegetables and cook. At eleven forty, she has already prepared the children's meals, and the old nanny sends the food away. Her husband always comes back at twelve fifteen, and of course, she takes care of lunch. After the meal, she reads the newspaper and chats with her husband. At two o'clock, her husband goes back to the factory, and she starts sewing or ironing clothes. At this time, the old nanny washes clothes. At three thirty, the old nanny still takes the children home, and she makes some snacks for them to eat. From four thirty to six o'clock, she supervises the children to study. At six fifteen, her husband returns home. Seven o'clock is dinner time. After dinner, she reads magazines and novels, or writes letters and records daily expenses. Her husband goes to visit neighbors and chat. At nine o'clock, they go to sleep. However, because the environment in Shanghai is corrupt, her husband sometimes has to go to the dance hall. Seeing this need, she also learns to dance. Within the possible range, she also does things in the society. She has a broad vision and a smart brain. She can manage the family according to the environment and teach the children according to the times. She does not have the habits of a Shanghai young lady at all. She never asks her husband to worry about the affairs of the family. Even if his income is not high, she can deal with it calmly. Except for her husband's suits and shirts and her own silk cheongsam, everything else is made by her own two hands. She has a thorough view of life, considerable knowledge, a kind attitude, and a hardworking spirit. The four words "standard wife" can truly be worthy of her.

Food Configuration for Worker Breastfeeding 246

— Zhang Yu

Cow's milk one pound (500 c.c.)

Sugar 5% of which half is water (1/5 pound 100cc or three taels of water in sugar)

Lactic acid forty-five to sixty drops (if more is needed, increase the side ratio; if not so much is needed, decrease the ratio.)

(Note) This type of milk should not be made with iron or lead utensils, because it can react chemically with lactic acid. The hand dripping lactic acid should be slow, and the hand mixing the milk should be fast, so that the lactic acid dripped down will not solidify the protein in the milk and form lumps.

Preparation of Milk Powder

Using milk powder instead of human milk has more drawbacks than fresh cow's milk. Because after cow's milk is dried into powder by heat and pressure, one of the vitamins in it is destroyed. There are many types of milk powder, and many mothers mistakenly believe in the merchants' propaganda and think it is so safe and happy to use it, which is the most dangerous. Milk powder can also be used for mothers with special diseases, and if it is not easy to get fresh cow's milk at home. The dosage can be based on the instructions of various milk powders. However, a few cc (C.C.) of orange juice or tomato juice, or tea, should be added to each breastfeed.

Feeding Method

The milk bottle should be round and have no concave corners for easy cleaning. Do not use bottles connected by leather tubes. The holes on the nipples should not be too large to prevent milk from entering the baby's mouth too quickly. After each feeding, the milk bottle and nipple must be washed, boiled, and stored properly. The temperature of the milk should be appropriate. Before each feeding, you can drop a little milk on the back of an adult's hand to test the temperature. When feeding, the milk should be directed towards the nipple to prevent air from being fed into the baby's stomach. After feeding, you can pick up the baby and place the baby's head on the adult's shoulder, hold it with one hand, and gently pat it with the other hand to expel the air that has entered the stomach, so as not to cause discomfort in the stomach. According to the above method, feed six or five times a day (once in the middle of the night can be reduced as appropriate due to sleep), once every four hours. The amount of milk should be determined according to the size of the baby. After it is slightly larger, other foods containing vitamins should be added.

Longde Lane 247

— Yin

It has been a long time since I went to the southern city. My experience in Longde Lane five years ago has gradually faded away like a photo that has been stored for too long. At first, we entrusted the entire family to house number thirty-four inside. I don't know who lives there now. People are really the most active things!

Less than half a month ago, I had to go through Xinbeimen and into Jiumu Land alone for the sake of the children in the family. The scenery on the street still retained some familiar traces, which made me involuntarily feel a very sincere old friendship. So, after finishing the business, I specially took a detour and bent to Longde Lane.

The red wall bricks have gradually faded into light yellow, and the painted alley doors have been peeled off like a patchwork coat worn by beggars. The small shops and shoe repair stalls at the entrance of the alley have also been replaced by new people. Only the Jiangbei people who watched the alley are still there and have not left.

My goal was originally to visit an old neighbor in house number thirty-five, a Suzhou young woman whose face was always yellow and thin, but very kind and loved to read books. But before I had walked to the door of house number thirty-five, the Jiangbei people who watched the alley had already shouted in a loud voice, "The Li family moved away long ago!"

Moving is a very common thing, of course, there is nothing surprising. However, the talkative Jiangbei people went on to automatically tell me the reason why his family moved away, which immediately made me feel infinitely sad.

The Li family was not a propertied class. Their lives depended entirely on Mr. Li's income from the telegraph office. However, they still had several relatives living with them. Everyone was very happy and lively, and they often held banquets and played cards, which was very extravagant. It really seemed like they were doing well. Only the Li family's wife still had some brains. She often told me behind their backs that the economy was very tight and that she absolutely hated this kind of extravagance. Unfortunately, her husband refused to listen to her and continued to mess around. This person originally had lung disease, and coupled with the day and night of messing around, the symptoms became more and more serious. He finally died of vomiting blood a year ago. Those relatives, seeing that they had no support, scattered and left, leaving the Li family's wife to take her two very young children back to the countryside in the cold. According to the Jiangbei people, the travel expenses back were only enough after selling many things. Those children were so thin that only a handful of bones remained. It seemed that they were also suffering from minor tuberculosis and could not live long.

When I walked out of Longde Lane, it still seemed like I could hear the sound of the Li family playing cards in my ears.

Page 19

Commentary

The Problem of Relieving Unemployed Youth 248

— Xing An

The unemployment problem of educated youth has now reached a serious stage. Every year, among the graduates of various schools across the country, except for a small number who have jobs, most of the rest suffer from the "graduation is unemployment" problem. As a result, not only the youth themselves feel bored, but also the society gradually shows signs of unrest. Recently, graduates of various universities in Beiping organized the "Service Movement Alliance" and held petitions, which is enough to show the seriousness of this problem.

In order to cope with the current major problems, the authorities have come up with various methods to relieve unemployed youth in order to solve the problem. The Executive Yuan has recently decided to do its best to select graduates from colleges and secondary schools: (1) The Yuan will consult with the Examination Yuan to hold a national college entrance examination once a year, and ask them to change the treatment as appropriate; (2) The government will hold colleges above the special college level in the Central Political School. Recent graduates who have not yet found employment will be given short-term training. and internships, after which they will be tested as appropriate, and the government will try to help them find employment; (3) At least 50,000 teachers and instructors are needed for the promotion of compulsory education and mass education in the 25th year, and most of them plan to select, train, and assign graduates from junior high schools and junior and senior normal schools who have not yet found employment. If these measures can be implemented one by one, the unemployment problem of educated youth will not be completely solved, but at least a part of the relief can be obtained.

However, we still have some opinions on the measures taken by the authorities to select graduates. Holding a national college entrance examination once a year is naturally a method of selecting talents. However, the national college entrance examination has been held in the past, and it is said that many of the successful candidates still do not have jobs. Therefore, it is important for the authorities to hold the national college entrance examination, and it is especially necessary to arrange as many jobs as possible for the successful candidates. Otherwise, only giving titles without giving jobs still loses the meaning of relieving unemployment. A piece of certificate cannot be eaten.

In the end, the authorities have established a preparatory committee for the employment guidance class for college graduates and above to carry out everything for training graduates. The training period is set at six months. The internship period is currently set at three to six months. During the training period, each person will receive a subsidy of 30 yuan. During the internship period, each person will receive a subsidy of 40 yuan. These measures are appropriate, but the number of students is only limited to 1,000 unemployed graduates from various schools in the past three years, which is too small. And those who graduated before three years have no opportunity to receive training, and the relief is also unfair. We hope that the authorities will expand the training class as much as possible so that more unemployed graduates have the opportunity to receive training and employment.

However, solving the unemployment problem of educated youth is not an easy task. Selecting graduates is only a temporary remedy. For further relief, we must start by reforming the current education system. The decline of the social economy is indeed a major reason for the unemployment of today's graduates, but the defects of the education system also make it so. The former Minister of Education reported that there are fewer unemployed youths studying practical subjects than those studying other subjects. We hope that the authorities will improve this. The Beiping University Graduates Service Movement Alliance has put forward suggestions: (1) reform the education system, (2) improve the examination system, (3) improve the standards for the appointment of local administrative personnel, (4) implement the national teacher system, (5) equalize salaries, and (6) strictly implement the evaluation and performance appraisal system, which are also ways to relieve unemployment, and we hope that the authorities will adopt them.

Fate 249

— Zheng Mingzi

(Fate is like a bottomless well, opening its fearful mouth in the dark world of night, as if containing a victorious pride in its sneer, waiting for the stumbling traveler!

So, another ordinary soul, in the green age, quietly sank into the dark and deep cave of fate.

There, there is no air, no clear water, no sunlight. People groped blindly, exploring, until old age, until death...)

Thinking back for a long time, it has been quite a while since I lived in this remote and desolate small village; the harvest is bad, and it has become common to hear the unpleasant quarrels and beatings of the villagers outside during the day; in the sleepless nights of deliberation, I hear some faint cries mixed with the sound of the clapper in the distance, and the next day, I hear that the husband or woman of that family jumped into the well or hanged themselves because they could not borrow rice! These have already become so common that they have lost the qualification to cause a stir. Everyone treats it as a common trivial matter: they listen to it, frown, then put it aside and no longer talk about it, and quickly forget it completely without paying attention. The people in the village are thus removed day by day? As ordinary as brushing away a speck of dust.

Because of this, when I heard the woman say that there was no rice left, and there was nothing to pawn, we all thought of the small river flowing with muddy water in front of the door, and the tall and sturdy branches that were enough to hang people to death.

(Dangerous, ominous and terrible thoughts!

Thinking so, I felt even more afraid: people who fall into the trap of fate should never have the hope of transcending life, right? Fate is cruel... But, fate! What exactly is it?

Maybe it's not destined to embrace life so broken? When I was in school, wasn't I a happy and lively young man? So, after three years of wandering melted people into a pile of broken pieces of decline, they came to live in this remote place with their heads upside down.

However, everything is the same bad! The broken pieces of life can no longer be sewn together! Even if I only receive a little insignificant news from acquaintances over the years, I will quickly think of the vast world outside and the fate floating in this vast world.

"Let's go to the outside world again and try to find a chance to live!" Thinking so, I pawned even the worthless furniture, regardless of whether I was sure or not, and regardless of the woman's hesitation; in order to find acquaintances, I had to make my face look good, and I had to prepare some painful gifts with the money from the pawn! Just for the sake of living, try the means of fate again?

A kind of sad mood floated up, and the woman and children were with me, like soldiers on an expedition, like beggars in exile. The sentences I saw in some books were deeply engraved in my memory;

"Recently, there is a lack of supply in the kitchen, and the baby is crying and the rice basket is empty; the mother whispers in the ear of the child: Daddy has a new poem to visit the minister!"

(Clearly, a tragedy exists in the world, like moldy moss: people have to use their own tears to provide laughter for others!)

Because of this, I forgot the past story of being played by fate, forgot my own tears, and blindly threw myself and two lives into the hands of unknown fate in the middle of no certainty. (What is knowable in this world?)

A river, a sailing ship, and a third-class cabin berth, carrying some uncertain lives, sailed quickly towards an even greater unknown. Tears need to be saved to exchange for people's laughter (I really dare not think about it!), and people's laughter will be the master of their own fate...

Everything is uncertain: in the confusion, in the noise of people, I saw the gray land, and took the woman and children, squeezed into a group of people with the same wandering, and stepped on the shore, which, it is said, is the metropolis! How beautiful are the roads in the metropolis:

Page 20

The woman paid three coppers to a fortune teller at the dock to ask about "the year's fortune", and when she walked to the street, she felt a little confused. Obviously: the black hand of unknown fate once again fell on my head.

The Big Fellow 250

— By One

It was not until the sun had set that the big fellow slowly, listlessly, dragged his weary steps homeward; but when he reached his doorway, he stopped, tormented by anguish, lacking the courage to push open the half-closed gate.

His brow was furrowed deeply, and in the dim twilight his gaunt face, ravaged by hunger, appeared even more pallid and terrifying. His sunken eyes stared blankly into space, and his constricted chest heaved violently—his ribs seemed about to pierce his thin skin. He gasped for breath, his limbs twitching weakly, exhausted from the day's toil. He leaned half his body against the peeling wall, seeking a moment's respite, recalling the day's painful encounters.

"I have no relatives, no friends! I..."

Suddenly, the big fellow slammed his fist against the mud wall, letting out a ragged cry that startled his sick wife inside, who erupted into a fit of violent dry coughing, the harsh rasping sounds audible even from outside. As if remembering something, the big fellow pushed himself off the wall, flung open the door, and rushed inside.

"How is it...Big Fellow..." his wife asked in a faint, weak voice laced with a desperate hope.

He didn't answer.

His wife broke into another fit of coughing.

"What the hell are you living for? You…you, living, living…you…!" The big fellow, like a maddened beast, lunged to his wife's bedside, grabbed her hair with one hand, and began beating her with the other.

She only gasped and coughed, offering no resistance as the big fellow struck her. She opened her mouth several times to speak, but the blows prevented her.

"It's because of you that I'm poor and miserable! You, you, you hurry up and die, you…!" The big fellow's fists rained down on his wife, again and again, as she silently endured the beating, collapsing into his arms. Finally, the big fellow could no longer strike; he stopped, tears streaming down his face. He suddenly began to sob, clutching his wife tightly. She smiled bitterly, reaching out a withered hand to wipe away his tears.

"Hit me, Big Fellow! ...I, I don't hate you, I hate myself for burdening you, I... I wish you would beat me to death..." The wife wept too.

"No, I was wrong, I shouldn't have hit you, you're sick..." The big fellow's tears fell on his wife's face. "I'm angry, I'm angry at those bastards, they're not human!..."

"What?...Didn't you go to the boss's place either?..."

"I went, I pleaded and begged him, asked him to lend me some money for food and to treat your illness... He refused...I knelt and kowtowed, but he still refused... Heartless! ...I used to work hard for him, but he's forgotten it all. I said I'd pay it back sooner or later, but he just gritted his teeth, unwilling to part with a single cent, and finally had people drag me out! ...Damn him! ...Beast! ...They even kicked me a few times! ...I'm angry, I'm…?..."

"Oh!...It would be better if I died, burdening you, I'm so sorry...Big Fellow!..."

"You can't die! You... I'll find a way, I..." He stretched out his thin hand, seemingly confident.

But no "solution" flew in through the window; nor did it leap in from outside the door. The big fellow's waving hand dropped, slowly hanging down. He looked out the window, into a sea of darkness.

Last Year's Nie Er Memorial Meeting at Jin Cheng Gate 255

Nie Er's Elegy 256

Sun Shiyi wrote the lyrics, Lü Ji created the score

The wind is calling, the sea is roaring, the waves are beckoning, when the night is deep, the moon is shining in the sky, young friends, he plunged into the embrace of the ocean; swallowed by the water's waves, the high tide. How could we have known? From now on, farewell forever! From now on, we have been deprived of our ambitious hero; from now on, we lack you at our front lines. From now on, where do you drift? The homeland is far away! From now on, remembering people thousands of miles away, only dreams are distant!

Great ambition is empty, hard work is not in vain, listening to thousands of people singing the heroic songs you composed, you should be smiling in the nine springs. Facing the shocking news, watching the boundless waves, do you know that the friends in the homeland, today, with broken hearts, are paying their respects to you?
